## 2.7 Note Taking & Documentation

### 2.7.1 Overview

**Purpose:** Capture thoughts, ideas, and information with a flexible, organized note-taking system.

**Target Users:** All users (80% expected adoption)

**Tier:** **FREE** (Core Feature)

**Key Differentiators:**
- Rich text editor with markdown support
- Organizational hierarchy (notebooks → notes)
- Quick capture from anywhere
- Search and tagging
- Media embedding
- Templates
- Version history (🔒 Premium)

### 2.7.2 Core Features

**Note Structure:**
```javascript
{
  id: "uuid",
  title: "Meeting Notes - Q1 Planning",
  content: "<rich text HTML or markdown>",
  contentType: "richtext|markdown|checklist",
  
  // Organization
  notebook: "notebookId",
  tags: ["meeting", "planning", "Q1"],
  category: "work",
  
  // Metadata
  createdDate: "2026-01-19T10:30:00Z",
  modifiedDate: "2026-01-19T14:45:00Z",
  author: "userId",
  
  // Features
  pinned: true,
  starred: false,
  archived: false,
  encrypted: false, // 🔒 Premium
  
  // Attachments
  attachments: ["fileId1", "fileId2"],
  images: ["imageId1"],
  
  // Connections
  linkedTasks: ["taskId1"],
  linkedEvents: ["eventId1"],
  linkedNotes: ["noteId2"], // backlinks
  
  // Sharing (future)
  shared: false,
  permissions: [],
  
  // Version control
  versionHistory: [] // 🔒 Premium
}
```

**Editor Features:**
- **Formatting:** Bold, italic, underline, strikethrough
- **Lists:** Bulleted, numbered, checklists
- **Headings:** H1-H6
- **Links:** URLs, internal note links
- **Code:** Inline code, code blocks with syntax highlighting
- **Tables:** Create and edit tables
- **Images:** Drag-drop, paste, upload
- **Embeds:** YouTube videos, tweets, maps
- **Mentions:** @task, @event references (🔒 Premium)

**Organization:**
- **Notebooks:** Top-level containers
- **Sections:** Within notebooks (🔒 Premium)
- **Tags:** Cross-cutting categorization
- **Favorites:** Pin important notes
- **Recently Viewed:** Quick access to recent notes

### 2.7.3 Note Templates

**Built-in Templates:**
- Meeting Notes (agenda, attendees, action items)
- Daily Journal (date, mood, highlights, reflections)
- Project Plan (goals, timeline, resources, risks)
- Book Summary (title, author, key points, quotes)
- Decision Log (context, options, decision, reasoning)
- Learning Notes (concept, examples, practice questions)

**Custom Templates (🔒 Premium):**
- Create your own
- Reusable structure
- Variables and placeholders

### 2.7.4 Search & Discovery

**Full-Text Search:**
- Search across all note content
- Filter by notebook, tag, date
- Search within attachments (🔒 Premium)
- Keyboard shortcut (Cmd/Ctrl + P)

**Smart Suggestions:**
- Related notes based on content
- Suggested tags
- Duplicate detection
- Orphaned notes (no tags, no notebook)

### 2.7.5 Collaboration (Future/Premium)

- Share notes with read/write permissions
- Real-time collaborative editing
- Comments and discussion threads
- Change tracking

### 2.7.6 User Flow

**Quick Note Creation:**
```
1. Press Cmd/Ctrl + N anywhere
2. New note window opens
3. Start typing title
4. Press Tab, begin content
5. Auto-saves as you type
6. Click outside or Cmd+S to finalize
7. Choose notebook (or default "Quick Notes")
8. Add tags if desired
9. Note saved
```

## 2.8 Health & Wellness Tracker

### 2.8.1 Overview

**Purpose:** Monitor health metrics and wellness indicators to understand mind-body connections with productivity.

**Target Users:** Wellness-focused users (40% expected adoption)

**Tier:** 🔒 **PREMIUM** ($4/month)

**Key Differentiators:**
- Multiple health metric tracking
- Integration with fitness devices (Apple Health, Google Fit)
- Correlation with productivity metrics
- Sleep tracking and analysis
- Mood and energy logging
- Insights on health-productivity relationships

### 2.8.2 Trackable Metrics

**Physical Health:**
- Weight and body composition
- Sleep duration and quality
- Exercise (type, duration, intensity)
- Water intake
- Nutrition (calories, macros)
- Heart rate, blood pressure
- Steps and movement

**Mental Wellness:**
- Mood (scale or emoji)
- Energy levels
- Stress levels
- Anxiety/depression indicators
- Mindfulness minutes

**Habits:**
- Caffeine consumption
- Alcohol intake
- Screen time
- Time outdoors

### 2.8.3 Data Entry

**Methods:**
- Manual daily logging
- Import from Apple Health
- Import from Google Fit
- Import from Fitbit, Garmin, etc.
- Smart scale integration
- Photo journaling

**Quick Log Interface:**
- Daily check-in form (2-3 minutes)
- Most important metrics prioritized
- Historical data visible for context
- Streaks and trends shown

### 2.8.4 Analytics

**Health Dashboard:**
- Key metrics overview
- Trends over time
- Averages and ranges
- Correlation insights

**Productivity Correlation:**
- "On days you sleep >7hrs, your productivity is 25% higher"
- "Exercise correlates with better mood scores"
- "High caffeine days show productivity spike then crash"

**Reports:**
- Weekly health summary
- Monthly trends
- Export data for doctor visits

## 2.9 Focus Timer (Pomodoro)

### 2.9.1 Overview

**Purpose:** Structured focus sessions using Pomodoro Technique and custom intervals to enhance concentration.

**Target Users:** Students, career professionals (45% expected adoption)

**Tier:** 🔒 **PREMIUM** ($3/month)

**Features:**
- Customizable work/break intervals
- Task integration (what are you working on?)
- Distraction logging
- Session statistics
- Ambient sound options
- Do Not Disturb mode integration

**Pomodoro Workflow:**
```
1. Choose task to work on
2. Start 25-minute focus timer
3. Work without interruptions
4. Timer ends, 5-minute break starts
5. After 4 pomodoros, 15-30 minute long break
6. Repeat cycle
7. Track completed pomodoros per task
```

**Customization:**
- Custom intervals (25/5 is default, adjust to preference)
- Auto-start next phase or manual
- Skip break option
- Extended break after X sessions
- Different profiles (deep work, light work, study)

**Integration:**
- Links to time tracking
- Counts toward task time estimates
- Productivity analytics

---

**Dashboard Widgets:**
- Today's summary (tasks, events, time, habits)

**AI Insights:**

- Productivity patterns identified
- Recommendations for improvement

- Predictive scheduling

**Reports:**

## 3.1 Inventory Management System

### 3.1.1 Overview

**Purpose:** Track inventory levels, manage stock across multiple locations, automate reordering, and prevent stockouts for product-based businesses.

**Target Users:** Retail businesses, e-commerce, manufacturing, warehouses (45% of enterprise users)

**Tier:** 🔒 **PREMIUM** ($75/month base + $2/user)

**Key Differentiators:**
- Multi-location inventory tracking
- Real-time stock level monitoring
- Automated low-stock alerts
- Barcode/QR code scanning
- Batch and lot tracking
- FIFO/LIFO/FEFO cost methods
- Integration with order management and accounting

### 3.1.2 Core Features

#### Product Management

**Product Schema:**
```javascript
{
  id: "uuid",
  sku: "PROD-001",
  name: "Wireless Mouse",
  description: "Ergonomic wireless mouse with USB receiver",
  
  // Classification
  category: "Electronics",
  subcategory: "Computer Accessories",
  brand: "TechBrand",
  tags: ["wireless", "ergonomic", "office"],
  
  // Variants
  hasVariants: true,
  variants: [
    {
      id: "var1",
      sku: "PROD-001-BLK",
      attributes: { color: "Black", size: "Standard" },
      barcode: "123456789012",
      stockLevel: 150
    },
    {
      id: "var2",
      sku: "PROD-001-WHT",
      attributes: { color: "White", size: "Standard" },
      barcode: "123456789013",
      stockLevel: 80
    }
  ],
  
  // Inventory Tracking
  trackInventory: true,
  inventoryMethod: "FIFO|LIFO|FEFO|Average",
  stockLevel: 230, // total across all variants/locations
  reservedStock: 15, // allocated to pending orders
  availableStock: 215,
  reorderPoint: 50,
  reorderQuantity: 100,
  safetyStock: 25,
  
  // Multi-location
  stockByLocation: [
    { locationId: "warehouse1", quantity: 150 },
    { locationId: "store1", quantity: 80 }
  ],
  
  // Batches/Lots
  batchTracking: true,
  batches: [
    {
      batchNumber: "BATCH-2026-001",
      quantity: 100,
      manufacturingDate: "2026-01-01",
      expiryDate: "2028-01-01",
      location: "warehouse1",
      cost: 8.50
    }
  ],
  
  // Pricing
  costPrice: 8.50,
  sellingPrice: 24.99,
  wholesalePrice: 18.99,
  margin: 194%, // calculated
  currency: "USD",
  taxable: true,
  taxRate: 0.08,
  
  // Physical Properties
  weight: 0.15, // kg
  dimensions: { length: 10, width: 6, height: 4 }, // cm
  
  // Supplier Info
  primarySupplier: "supplierId",
  supplierSKU: "SUP-WM-001",
  leadTime: 14, // days
  moq: 50, // minimum order quantity
  
  // Images & Media
  images: ["imageId1", "imageId2"],
  documents: ["specSheet.pdf"],
  
  // Status
  status: "active|discontinued|out_of_stock",
  createdDate: "2025-06-01",
  lastRestocked: "2026-01-15",
  
  // Audit
  createdBy: "userId",
  lastModifiedBy: "userId",
  lastModifiedDate: "2026-01-19"
}
```

#### Stock Operations

**Stock Movements:**
```javascript
{
  id: "uuid",
  type: "adjustment|received|sold|transferred|returned|damaged|lost",
  productId: "productId",
  variantId: "variantId",
  batchNumber: "BATCH-2026-001",
  
  quantity: 50,
  quantityBefore: 180,
  quantityAfter: 230,
  
  fromLocation: "supplierId", // for received
  toLocation: "warehouse1",
  
  date: "2026-01-19",
  reason: "Purchase order #PO-1234 received",
  notes: "Checked and verified",
  
  relatedDocument: {
    type: "purchase_order|sale|transfer|adjustment",
    id: "documentId"
  },
  
  costPerUnit: 8.50,
  totalCost: 425.00,
  
  performedBy: "userId",
  approvedBy: "managerId",
  
  attachments: ["deliveryNote.pdf"]
}
```

**Operation Types:**

1. **Stock Adjustment:** Manual correction of inventory levels
2. **Stock Receipt:** Receiving inventory from suppliers
3. **Stock Sale:** Inventory sold to customers (auto from orders)
4. **Stock Transfer:** Moving between locations
5. **Stock Return:** Customer returns or supplier returns
6. **Stock Damage/Loss:** Write-offs and losses

#### Alerts & Automation

**Automated Alerts:**
- **Low Stock Alert:** When inventory drops below reorder point
- **Out of Stock:** When quantity reaches zero
- **Overstock Alert:** When inventory exceeds maximum threshold
- **Expiry Warning:** Products approaching expiration (30/60/90 days)
- **Slow-Moving Stock:** Items not sold in X days
- **Dead Stock:** No movement in 180+ days

**Auto-Reordering (🔒 Premium Plus):**
- Automatic purchase order generation when stock hits reorder point
- Smart reorder quantity calculation based on:
  - Historical sales velocity
  - Lead time
  - Safety stock requirements
  - Seasonal trends
- Send to supplier or require approval

**Stock Forecasting:**
- Predict future stock needs based on:
  - Historical sales data
  - Seasonality patterns
  - Growth trends
  - Upcoming promotions
- Recommend optimal stock levels

#### Multi-Location Management

**Locations:**
- **Warehouses:** Primary storage facilities
- **Retail Stores:** Physical store locations
- **Consignment:** Stock at partner locations
- **In-Transit:** Stock being transferred

**Location Features:**
- Real-time stock visibility across all locations
- Transfer requests between locations
- Location-specific reorder points
- Stock allocation rules (which location fulfills orders)
- Location performance analytics

#### Barcode & Scanning

**Supported Formats:**
- UPC/EAN barcodes
- QR codes
- Custom SKU codes

**Scanning Functions:**
- Stock receiving (scan to add)
- Stock counting (physical inventory)
- Order fulfillment (scan to ship)
- Product lookup
- Mobile app barcode scanner

**Physical Inventory:**
- Scheduled or ad-hoc stock counts
- Count sheets generation
- Variance reports (expected vs. actual)
- Adjustment recommendations
- Count history and accuracy tracking

### 3.1.3 Reports & Analytics

**Inventory Reports:**
- **Current Stock Report:** Real-time inventory levels
- **Stock Valuation:** Total inventory value (at cost)
- **Stock Movement Report:** All transactions in date range
- **Reorder Report:** Items needing reorder
- **Dead Stock Report:** Non-moving inventory
- **ABC Analysis:** Categorize inventory by value/velocity
- **Stock Aging Report:** How long items have been in stock

**Performance Metrics:**
- Inventory turnover ratio
- Days inventory outstanding
- Stock accuracy rate
- Fill rate (demand met from stock)
- Carrying cost of inventory

---

## 3.2 Order Management System

### 3.2.1 Overview

**Purpose:** End-to-end order processing from creation to fulfillment, integrated with inventory and customer management.

**Target Users:** E-commerce, retail, wholesale, B2B (70% of enterprise users)

**Tier:** 🔒 **PREMIUM** ($60/month base + $1.50/user)

**Key Differentiators:**
- Multi-channel order consolidation
- Automated fulfillment workflows
- Real-time order tracking
- Integration with shipping carriers
- Returns and refunds management
- B2B and wholesale order support

### 3.2.2 Core Features

#### Order Schema

```javascript
{
  id: "uuid",
  orderNumber: "ORD-2026-00123",
  type: "sales_order|purchase_order|transfer_order",
  
  // Customer Info
  customer: {
    id: "customerId",
    name: "John Doe",
    email: "john@example.com",
    phone: "+1-555-0123",
    type: "retail|wholesale|b2b"
  },
  
  // Order Details
  items: [
    {
      productId: "productId",
      variantId: "variantId",
      sku: "PROD-001-BLK",
      name: "Wireless Mouse - Black",
      quantity: 2,
      unitPrice: 24.99,
      discount: 0,
      tax: 4.00,
      total: 53.98
    }
  ],
  
  // Pricing
  subtotal: 49.98,
  discountTotal: 0,
  taxTotal: 4.00,
  shippingCost: 8.99,
  totalAmount: 62.97,
  currency: "USD",
  
  // Addresses
  billingAddress: {
    street: "123 Main St",
    city: "New York",
    state: "NY",
    zipCode: "10001",
    country: "USA"
  },
  shippingAddress: { /* same structure */ },
  
  // Fulfillment
  fulfillmentStatus: "pending|processing|packed|shipped|delivered|cancelled",
  paymentStatus: "pending|authorized|paid|refunded|failed",
  
  warehouse: "warehouse1",
  shippingMethod: "standard|express|overnight",
  carrier: "UPS|FedEx|USPS",
  trackingNumber: "1Z999AA10123456784",
  
  // Dates
  orderDate: "2026-01-19T10:30:00Z",
  expectedShipDate: "2026-01-20",
  expectedDeliveryDate: "2026-01-25",
  actualShipDate: null,
  actualDeliveryDate: null,
  
  // Payment
  paymentMethod: "credit_card|debit_card|paypal|bank_transfer|cash",
  paymentReference: "ch_1234567890",
  
  // Source
  channel: "website|mobile_app|in_store|phone|marketplace",
  salesPerson: "userId",
  
  // Notes
  customerNotes: "Please gift wrap",
  internalNotes: "VIP customer",
  
  // Related
  invoiceId: "invoiceId",
  shipmentId: "shipmentId",
  
  // Status History
  statusHistory: [
    { status: "pending", timestamp: "2026-01-19T10:30:00Z", user: "system" },
    { status: "processing", timestamp: "2026-01-19T11:00:00Z", user: "userId" }
  ]
}
```

#### Order Workflow

**Order Lifecycle:**
```
1. Order Created
   ↓
2. Payment Authorized/Received
   ↓
3. Inventory Reserved
   ↓
4. Order Processing (picking items)
   ↓
5. Order Packed
   ↓
6. Shipping Label Generated
   ↓
7. Order Shipped
   ↓
8. In Transit
   ↓
9. Delivered
   ↓
10. Order Completed
```

**Automated Actions:**
- **On Order Creation:**
  - Reserve inventory
  - Send order confirmation email to customer
  - Notify fulfillment team
  - Check fraud risk (high-value orders)

- **On Payment Received:**
  - Update payment status
  - Trigger fulfillment workflow
  - Update accounting records

- **On Shipment:**
  - Send tracking email to customer
  - Update inventory (deduct stock)
  - Create invoice

- **On Delivery:**
  - Request review/feedback
  - Close order
  - Archive

#### Multi-Channel Support

**Sales Channels:**
- **Direct Website:** Native e-commerce integration
- **Mobile App:** In-app purchases
- **In-Store POS:** Physical store sales
- **Phone Orders:** Manual entry by staff
- **Marketplaces:** Amazon, eBay, Etsy (🔒 Premium Plus)
- **Wholesale Portal:** B2B customer orders

**Channel Features:**
- Unified order view across all channels
- Channel-specific pricing rules
- Inventory sync across channels
- Channel performance analytics

#### Fulfillment Management

**Picking & Packing:**
- Pick lists generation (optimized by warehouse layout)
- Batch picking for multiple orders
- Packing slips printing
- Quality check workflow
- Gift wrapping options

**Shipping Integration (🔒 Premium):**
- Real-time rate calculation from carriers
- Label generation (UPS, FedEx, USPS, DHL)
- Tracking number auto-import
- Shipment notifications
- Batch shipping for multiple orders
- International customs forms

**Drop Shipping:**
- Forward orders to suppliers
- Supplier fulfillment tracking
- Automated supplier notifications

#### Returns & Refunds

**Return Management:**
```javascript
{
  id: "uuid",
  returnNumber: "RET-2026-00045",
  orderId: "orderId",
  customer: "customerId",
  
  items: [
    {
      orderItemId: "itemId",
      productId: "productId",
      quantityReturned: 1,
      reason: "defective|wrong_item|not_as_described|changed_mind",
      condition: "unopened|opened|damaged",
      restockable: true
    }
  ],
  
  refundAmount: 24.99,
  refundShipping: true,
  restockingFee: 0,
  
  status: "requested|approved|received|refunded|rejected",
  
  returnLabel: "labelId",
  trackingNumber: "9876543210",
  
  notes: "Product arrived damaged in shipping",
  photos: ["photo1.jpg", "photo2.jpg"],
  
  requestDate: "2026-01-25",
  approvedDate: "2026-01-25",
  receivedDate: null,
  refundedDate: null
}
```

**Return Workflow:**
1. Customer requests return
2. Admin reviews and approves/rejects
3. Return label generated and emailed
4. Customer ships item back
5. Warehouse receives and inspects
6. If approved: Restock inventory + issue refund
7. If rejected: Return to customer with explanation

**Refund Processing:**
- Full refunds
- Partial refunds
- Store credit option
- Restocking fees (configurable)
- Automatic or manual approval

### 3.2.3 Order Analytics

**Key Metrics:**
- Orders per day/week/month
- Average order value (AOV)
- Order fulfillment time
- Shipping time
- Return rate
- Order accuracy rate
- Revenue by channel

**Reports:**
- Sales by product
- Sales by customer segment
- Geographic sales distribution
- Peak ordering times
- Abandoned orders (started but not completed)

---

## 3.3 Finance & Accounting Suite

### 3.3.1 Overview

**Purpose:** Complete financial management including accounts, general ledger, expenses, revenue tracking, and financial reporting for small businesses.

**Target Users:** All enterprise users (85% adoption)

**Tier:** 🔒 **PREMIUM** ($80/month base + $3/user)

**Key Differentiators:**
- Double-entry accounting system
- Multi-currency support
- Automated reconciliation
- Financial statement generation
- Tax preparation support
- Integration with banking and payments
- Audit trail and compliance

### 3.3.2 Core Features

#### Chart of Accounts

**Account Structure:**
```javascript
{
  id: "uuid",
  accountNumber: "1000",
  accountName: "Cash - Operating Account",
  accountType: "asset|liability|equity|revenue|expense",
  accountSubtype: "current_asset|fixed_asset|current_liability|equity|operating_revenue|cogs|operating_expense",
  
  parentAccount: null, // for sub-accounts
  
  balance: 15250.50,
  currency: "USD",
  
  description: "Primary business checking account",
  taxRelevant: true,
  
  status: "active|inactive",
  
  bankAccountLinked: true,
  bankAccountId: "bankId",
  
  lastReconciled: "2026-01-15"
}
```

**Standard Chart of Accounts:**
```
Assets (1000-1999)
├─ Current Assets (1000-1299)
│  ├─ Cash & Cash Equivalents (1000-1099)
│  ├─ Accounts Receivable (1100-1199)
│  └─ Inventory (1200-1299)
└─ Fixed Assets (1300-1999)
   ├─ Property & Equipment (1300-1399)
   └─ Accumulated Depreciation (1400-1499)

Liabilities (2000-2999)
├─ Current Liabilities (2000-2299)
│  ├─ Accounts Payable (2000-2099)
│  ├─ Credit Cards (2100-2199)
│  └─ Short-term Loans (2200-2299)
└─ Long-term Liabilities (2300-2999)

Equity (3000-3999)
├─ Owner's Equity (3000-3099)
├─ Retained Earnings (3100-3199)
└─ Draws (3200-3299)

Revenue (4000-4999)
├─ Operating Revenue (4000-4499)
└─ Other Income (4500-4999)

Expenses (5000-9999)
├─ Cost of Goods Sold (5000-5999)
├─ Operating Expenses (6000-8999)
└─ Other Expenses (9000-9999)
```

#### Journal Entries

**Transaction Entry:**
```javascript
{
  id: "uuid",
  journalEntryNumber: "JE-2026-00123",
  date: "2026-01-19",
  type: "standard|adjusting|closing|reversing",
  
  description: "Payment received from customer",
  reference: "INV-2026-00045",
  
  lines: [
    {
      account: "1000", // Cash
      debit: 1000.00,
      credit: 0,
      description: "Payment from ABC Corp"
    },
    {
      account: "1100", // Accounts Receivable
      debit: 0,
      credit: 1000.00,
      description: "Invoice #45 settled"
    }
  ],
  
  totalDebit: 1000.00,
  totalCredit: 1000.00,
  balanced: true,
  
  source: "manual|automatic|import",
  sourceDocument: {
    type: "invoice|bill|order|payment",
    id: "documentId"
  },
  
  posted: true,
  postedDate: "2026-01-19T14:30:00Z",
  postedBy: "userId",
  
  attachments: ["receipt.pdf"],
  
  tags: ["customer_payment", "revenue"],
  
  approvalRequired: false,
  approvedBy: null,
  
  reversed: false,
  reversingEntry: null
}
```

**Automated Journal Entries:**
- Sales orders → Revenue recognition
- Purchase orders → Expense recognition
- Payroll → Salary expense
- Inventory movements → COGS adjustments
- Depreciation schedules
- Recurring entries (rent, subscriptions)

#### Accounts Receivable (AR)

**Customer Invoices:**
- Create and send professional invoices
- Recurring invoices for subscriptions
- Payment terms (Net 30, Net 60, etc.)
- Partial payments tracking
- Overdue notices automation
- Aging reports (current, 30, 60, 90+ days)

**Payment Collection:**
- Record payments against invoices
- Multiple payment methods
- Payment plans for large amounts
- Bad debt write-offs
- Collection reminders

#### Accounts Payable (AP)

**Vendor Bills:**
- Record bills from suppliers
- Payment scheduling
- Batch payments
- Early payment discounts
- 1099 tracking (US)

**Expense Management:**
- Employee expense claims
- Receipt scanning and OCR
- Approval workflows
- Reimbursement processing
- Expense categorization

#### Banking & Reconciliation

**Bank Feeds (🔒 Premium Plus):**
- Auto-import transactions from banks
- Smart categorization with ML
- Duplicate detection
- Match transactions to invoices/bills

**Bank Reconciliation:**
- Monthly reconciliation workflow
- Statement upload
- Match transactions
- Identify discrepancies
- Reconciliation reports
- Audit trail

#### Financial Statements

**Balance Sheet:**
- Assets = Liabilities + Equity
- Current vs. non-current classification
- Comparative periods
- Export to PDF/Excel

**Profit & Loss Statement (Income Statement):**
- Revenue - Expenses = Net Income
- Operating vs. non-operating income/expenses
- Gross profit, operating profit, net profit
- Month/quarter/year views
- YoY comparisons

**Cash Flow Statement:**
- Operating activities
- Investing activities
- Financing activities
- Beginning and ending cash
- Direct or indirect method

**Other Reports:**
- Trial Balance
- General Ledger
- Account Activity
- Budget vs. Actual
- Tax Summary

#### Budgeting & Forecasting

**Budget Management:**
- Create annual/monthly budgets by account
- Department/project budgets
- Budget vs. actual variance analysis
- Budget alerts and notifications
- Rolling forecasts

**Financial Planning:**
- Revenue projections
- Expense forecasting
- Cash flow projections
- Scenario modeling (best/worst/likely)

#### Multi-Currency

**Features:**
- Record transactions in any currency
- Automatic exchange rate updates
- Realized and unrealized gains/losses
- Multi-currency reporting
- Base currency conversion

#### Tax Management

**Tax Tracking:**
- Sales tax calculation and tracking
- Tax liability accounts
- Tax payment scheduling
- Form preparation assistance (1099, W-2, etc.)
- Tax reports for CPA

**Compliance:**
- Audit trail for all transactions
- User activity logs
- Read-only archive periods
- Data export for auditors

## 3.4 Employee Time & Attendance Tracking

### 3.4.1 Overview

**Purpose:** Track employee work hours, attendance, time-off, and integrate with payroll processing.

**Target Users:** All enterprise users with employees (90% adoption)

**Tier:** **FREE** (Core Feature, advanced features premium)

**Key Differentiators:**
- Multiple clock-in methods (web, mobile, kiosk)
- GPS and geofencing
- Shift scheduling
- Time-off management
- Overtime calculation
- Payroll integration
- Compliance reporting

### 3.4.2 Core Features

#### Time Tracking

**Clock In/Out:**
```javascript
{
  id: "uuid",
  employee: {
    id: "employeeId",
    name: "Jane Smith",
    employeeNumber: "EMP-001",
    department: "Sales",
    position: "Sales Associate"
  },
  
  clockInTime: "2026-01-19T09:00:00Z",
  clockOutTime: "2026-01-19T17:30:00Z",
  
  clockInMethod: "web|mobile|kiosk|manual",
  clockInLocation: {
    lat: 40.7128,
    lng: -74.0060,
    address: "123 Office St, New York, NY"
  },
  
  breakStart: "2026-01-19T12:00:00Z",
  breakEnd: "2026-01-19T12:30:00Z",
  
  totalHours: 8.0,
  regularHours: 8.0,
  overtimeHours: 0,
  breakTime: 0.5,
  
  scheduledShift: "shiftId",
  late: false,
  earlyLeave: false,
  
  workLocation: "office|remote|client_site",
  project: "projectId", // if working on specific project
  
  notes: "Worked on client presentation",
  
  approved: true,
  approvedBy: "managerId",
  approvedDate: "2026-01-20"
}
```

**Clock-In Methods:**

1. **Web App:** Desktop browser clock in/out
2. **Mobile App:** Smartphone with GPS verification
3. **Kiosk Mode:** Tablet at office entrance with PIN/photo
4. **Biometric:** Fingerprint/face recognition (hardware integration)
5. **Manual Entry:** Manager enters time for employees
6. **Auto Clock-In:** Based on location/device (🔒 Premium)

#### Geofencing & GPS

**Location Verification:**
- Define geofence around office/job sites
- Require employees within geofence to clock in
- GPS coordinates logged with each clock-in
- Prevent buddy punching
- Remote work tracking

#### Shift Scheduling

**Schedule Management:**
```javascript
{
  id: "uuid",
  employee: "employeeId",
  
  shiftDate: "2026-01-20",
  startTime: "09:00",
  endTime: "17:00",
  
  shiftType: "regular|overtime|on_call|remote",
  department: "Sales",
  location: "Main Office",
  
  breakDuration: 30, // minutes
  
  role: "Sales Associate",
  supervisor: "managerId",
  
  status: "scheduled|confirmed|missed|worked",
  
  notes: "Bring laptop for remote setup",
  
  createdBy: "managerId",
  createdDate: "2026-01-15"
}
```

**Scheduling Features:**
- Drag-and-drop calendar interface
- Recurring shifts
- Shift templates
- Auto-scheduling based on availability
- Shift swapping (employee-initiated, manager-approved)
- Coverage requirements monitoring
- Conflict detection (double-booking, overtime limits)

#### Time-Off Management

**Leave Request:**
```javascript
{
  id: "uuid",
  employee: "employeeId",
  
  leaveType: "vacation|sick|personal|parental|unpaid|bereavement",
  
  startDate: "2026-02-01",
  endDate: "2026-02-05",
  
  totalDays: 5,
  totalHours: 40,
  
  reason: "Family vacation",
  
  status: "pending|approved|denied|cancelled",
  
  requestedDate: "2026-01-19",
  reviewedBy: "managerId",
  reviewedDate: "2026-01-20",
  reviewNotes: "Approved - enjoy your trip!",
  
  affectsPayroll: true,
  paid: true
}
```

**Leave Policies:**
- Accrual rules (X days per year)
- Carry-over policies
- Blackout dates (no time-off periods)
- Minimum notice requirements
- Maximum consecutive days
- Balance tracking
- Automatic accrual calculations

#### Attendance Reports

**Reports:**
- **Timesheet Report:** Individual or team timesheets
- **Attendance Summary:** Who's in/out today
- **Late/Absence Report:** Tardiness and absences
- **Overtime Report:** OT hours by employee
- **Time-Off Report:** Leave taken and balances
- **Labor Cost Report:** Hours × wages
- **Department Hours:** Total hours by department
- **Payroll Export:** Ready for payroll processing

**Analytics:**
- Average hours per employee
- Absenteeism rate
- Overtime trends
- Peak staffing hours
- Schedule adherence

#### Payroll Integration

**Payroll Data Export:**
- Regular hours
- Overtime hours
- Holiday pay
- Sick/vacation hours used
- Custom pay codes
- Format: CSV, Excel, or direct integration with payroll software

**Supported Payroll Systems:**
- QuickBooks Payroll
- Gusto
- ADP
- Paychex
- Custom exports

## 3.5 Project Management & Collaboration

### 3.5.1 Overview

**Purpose:** Plan, execute, and track projects with team collaboration, task assignment, and progress monitoring.

**Target Users:** All enterprise users (95% adoption)

**Tier:** **FREE** (Core Feature, advanced features premium)

**Key Differentiators:**
- Multiple project views (list, board, Gantt, calendar)
- Task dependencies and critical path
- Resource allocation
- Team collaboration features
- Time tracking integration
- File sharing and version control
- Agile and waterfall methodologies

### 3.5.2 Core Features

#### Project Structure

**Project Schema:**
```javascript
{
  id: "uuid",
  projectCode: "PROJ-2026-001",
  name: "Website Redesign",
  description: "Complete redesign of company website",
  
  // Organization
  portfolio: "portfolioId", // group of related projects
  client: "clientId",
  
  // Methodology
  methodology: "agile|waterfall|hybrid",
  framework: "scrum|kanban|custom",
  
  // Team
  projectManager: "userId",
  team: [
    {
      userId: "userId1",
      role: "Developer",
      allocation: 100, // percentage
      hourlyRate: 75.00 // for cost tracking
    }
  ],
  
  // Timeline
  startDate: "2026-01-15",
  endDate: "2026-04-15",
  status: "planning|active|on_hold|completed|cancelled",
  
  // Budget
  budgetType: "fixed|time_and_materials",
  estimatedHours: 400,
  actualHours: 120,
  budgetAmount: 30000,
  actualCost: 9000,
  
  // Progress
  progress: 30, // percentage
  tasksTotal: 45,
  tasksCompleted: 14,
  
  // Milestones
  milestones: [
    {
      id: "m1",
      name: "Design Approval",
      dueDate: "2026-02-15",
      completed: true,
      completedDate: "2026-02-10"
    }
  ],
  
  // Settings
  visibility: "team|company|client",
  archived: false,
  
  // Metadata
  tags: ["marketing", "digital", "high_priority"],
  customFields: {
    "client_budget": 35000,
    "contract_number": "CNT-2026-045"
  }
}
```

#### Task Management (Enhanced from Individual)

**Team Task Schema:**
```javascript
{
  // All individual task properties plus:
  
  projectId: "projectId",
  
  assignedTo: "userId",
  assignedBy: "managerId",
  assignedDate: "2026-01-19",
  
  watchers: ["userId2", "userId3"], // notified of changes
  
  dependencies: [
    {
      taskId: "taskId2",
      type: "finish_to_start|start_to_start|finish_to_finish|start_to_finish",
      lag: 2 // days delay after dependency completes
    }
  ],
  
  estimatedHours: 8,
  actualHours: 6.5,
  
  billable: true,
  billingStatus: "not_invoiced|invoiced|paid",
  
  sprint: "sprintId", // for agile projects
  epicId: "epicId",
  storyPoints: 5, // agile estimation
  
  customStatus: "todo|in_review|qa|done", // customizable workflow
  
  comments: [
    {
      id: "commentId",
      user: "userId",
      text: "Design mockup attached",
      timestamp: "2026-01-19T15:30:00Z",
      attachments: ["mockup.png"]
    }
  ],
  
  timeEntries: ["timeEntryId1", "timeEntryId2"]
}
```

#### Project Views

**1. List View:**
- Hierarchical task list
- Group by: Status, Assignee, Priority, Milestone
- Filters and saved views
- Inline editing
- Bulk actions

**2. Board View (Kanban):**
- Customizable columns (To Do, In Progress, Review, Done)
- Drag-and-drop task movement
- WIP (work in progress) limits
- Swim lanes (by assignee, priority)
- Board for each project or cross-project boards

**3. Gantt Chart (🔒 Premium):**
- Timeline visualization
- Task dependencies shown
- Critical path highlighting
- Drag to adjust dates
- Milestone markers
- Resource allocation bars
- Baseline comparison (planned vs. actual)

**4. Calendar View:**
- Tasks plotted by due date
- Color-coded by project/priority
- Team calendar (who's working on what when)
- Drag to reschedule

**5. Timeline View:**
- High-level project roadmap
- Milestone-focused
- Multiple projects on one timeline
- Dependency arrows

#### Agile Features (🔒 Premium)

**Sprints:**
```javascript
{
  id: "uuid",
  sprintNumber: 5,
  name: "Sprint 5 - Authentication Module",
  project: "projectId",
  
  startDate: "2026-01-20",
  endDate: "2026-02-02",
  duration: 14, // days
  
  goal: "Complete user authentication and authorization",
  
  tasks: ["taskId1", "taskId2"],
  totalStoryPoints: 34,
  completedStoryPoints: 0,
  
  status: "planned|active|completed",
  
  dailyStandups: [
    {
      date: "2026-01-20",
      notes: "Team synced on sprint goals",
      attendees: ["userId1", "userId2"]
    }
  ],
  
  retrospective: {
    whatWentWell: "Good collaboration",
    whatToImprove: "Better estimation",
    actionItems: ["Use planning poker"]
  }
}
```

**Backlog Management:**
- Product backlog
- Sprint backlog
- Backlog grooming/refinement
- Priority ordering
- Story point estimation
- Epics and user stories

**Scrum Ceremonies:**
- Sprint planning
- Daily standups
- Sprint review
- Sprint retrospective
- Backlog refinement

**Burn Charts:**
- Burndown chart (work remaining)
- Burnup chart (work completed)
- Velocity tracking (story points per sprint)

#### Team Collaboration

**Comments & Mentions:**
- Comment on tasks, projects, documents
- @mention team members (notifications)
- Rich text comments
- File attachments
- Emoji reactions

**Activity Feed:**
- Real-time updates on project activity
- Filter by: All, Mentions, Assignments, Comments
- Mark as read/unread
- Email digests (daily/weekly)

**Notifications:**
- Task assigned to you
- Task deadline approaching
- Project milestone completed
- Mentioned in comment
- Task status changed
- New file uploaded

#### File Management

**Project Files:**
- Folder structure within projects
- Drag-drop upload
- File versioning
- Preview for common formats (PDF, images, Office docs)
- Attach files to tasks
- Shared drive per project

**Version Control:**
- Track file versions
- Restore previous versions
- See who changed what when
- Compare versions

#### Templates

**Project Templates:**
- Save projects as templates
- Pre-configured tasks, milestones, workflows
- Templates for common project types:
  - Software development
  - Marketing campaigns
  - Product launches
  - Event planning

**Task Templates:**
- Recurring task sets
- Checklists
- Standard operating procedures

### 3.5.3 Resource Management

**Resource Allocation:**
- View team capacity
- Assign resources to projects/tasks
- Prevent over-allocation
- Balance workload across team
- Resource utilization reports

**Capacity Planning:**
- Available hours per person
- Allocated hours
- Remaining capacity
- Forecast future resource needs

## 3.6 Customer Relationship Management (CRM)

### 3.6.1 Overview

**Purpose:** Manage customer relationships, track sales pipeline, and improve customer engagement.

**Target Users:** Sales-focused businesses (60% of enterprise users)

**Tier:** 🔒 **PREMIUM** ($65/month base + $2/user)

**Key Differentiators:**
- 360° customer view
- Sales pipeline visualization
- Lead scoring and qualification
- Email integration and tracking
- Activity timeline
- Reporting and forecasting

### 3.6.2 Core Features

#### Contact Management

**Contact Schema:**
```javascript
{
  id: "uuid",
  type: "lead|contact|customer",
  
  // Personal Info
  firstName: "John",
  lastName: "Doe",
  email: "john.doe@example.com",
  phone: "+1-555-0123",
  mobile: "+1-555-0124",
  
  // Company (for B2B)
  company: {
    id: "companyId",
    name: "Acme Corp",
    industry: "Technology",
    size: "50-200",
    website: "acmecorp.com",
    address: { /* full address */ }
  },
  
  position: "CTO",
  department: "Technology",
  
  // Lead Source
  source: "website|referral|cold_call|event|advertising|partner",
  sourceDetails: "Google Ads - Product Campaign",
  
  // Status
  status: "new|contacted|qualified|unqualified|customer|lost",
  leadScore: 85, // 0-100
  
  // Assignment
  owner: "salesRepId",
  team: "teamId",
  
  // Relationships
  deals: ["dealId1", "dealId2"],
  orders: ["orderId1"],
  invoices: ["invoiceId1"],
  
  // Communication
  activities: ["activityId1"], // calls, emails, meetings
  lastContactedDate: "2026-01-15",
  nextFollowUpDate: "2026-01-25",
  
  // Preferences
  communicationPreference: "email|phone|sms",
  doNotContact: false,
  emailOptIn: true,
  
  // Custom Fields
  customFields: {
    "budget": 50000,
    "decision_timeline": "Q1 2026",
    "pain_points": "Manual processes"
  },
  
  // Social
  linkedin: "linkedin.com/in/johndoe",
  twitter: "@johndoe",
  
  // Tags
  tags: ["enterprise", "hot_lead", "decision_maker"],
  
  // Notes
  notes: "Very interested in enterprise plan",
  
  // Metadata
  createdDate: "2026-01-10",
  createdBy: "userId",
  lastModifiedDate: "2026-01-19"
}
```

#### Sales Pipeline

**Deal/Opportunity Schema:**
```javascript
{
  id: "uuid",
  dealName: "Acme Corp - Enterprise Plan",
  
  contact: "contactId",
  company: "companyId",
  
  // Pipeline
  pipeline: "pipelineId",
  stage: "stageId",
  stageHistory: [
    { stage: "Prospecting", enteredDate: "2026-01-10", exitDate: "2026-01-12" },
    { stage: "Qualification", enteredDate: "2026-01-12", exitDate: null }
  ],
  
  // Value
  dealValue: 50000,
  currency: "USD",
  
  // Probability
  probability: 60, // percentage (auto or manual)
  expectedRevenue: 30000, // dealValue × probability
  
  // Timeline
  expectedCloseDate: "2026-03-31",
  actualCloseDate: null,
  
  // Status
  status: "open|won|lost",
  lostReason: null,
  
  // Assignment
  owner: "salesRepId",
  
  // Products
  products: [
    {
      productId: "productId",
      quantity: 10,
      unitPrice: 5000,
      discount: 0,
      total: 50000
    }
  ],
  
  // Activities
  activities: ["activityId1"],
  nextActivity: {
    type: "call",
    dueDate: "2026-01-22",
    description: "Product demo"
  },
  
  // Competitors
  competitors: ["Competitor A", "Competitor B"],
  
  // Notes
  notes: "Decision maker is CTO. Budget approved for Q1.",
  
  // Source
  source: "Inbound lead from website",
  
  createdDate: "2026-01-10",
  lastActivityDate: "2026-01-19"
}
```

**Pipeline Stages:**
```
Default Sales Pipeline:
1. Lead Generation (10% probability)
2. Qualification (20%)
3. Needs Analysis (40%)
4. Proposal (60%)
5. Negotiation (80%)
6. Closed Won (100%) or Closed Lost (0%)
```

**Custom Pipelines:**
- Create multiple pipelines (e.g., Enterprise Sales, SMB Sales, Partnership)
- Custom stages per pipeline
- Automation rules (e.g., auto-move after 30 days)

#### Activity Tracking

**Activity Types:**
```javascript
{
  id: "uuid",
  type: "call|email|meeting|task|note|demo",
  
  subject: "Product demo with Acme Corp",
  description: "Demonstrated enterprise features",
  
  relatedTo: {
    contact: "contactId",
    company: "companyId",
    deal: "dealId"
  },
  
  participants: ["contactId", "userId"],
  
  dueDate: "2026-01-19T14:00:00Z",
  completedDate: "2026-01-19T15:30:00Z",
  
  duration: 90, // minutes
  
  outcome: "positive|neutral|negative",
  nextSteps: "Send proposal by Friday",
  
  owner: "salesRepId",
  
  status: "scheduled|completed|cancelled"
}
```

**Email Integration (🔒 Premium):**
- Sync emails with contacts
- Email tracking (opens, clicks)
- Email templates
- Bulk email campaigns
- Auto-log emails to CRM

#### Lead Management

**Lead Capture:**
- Web forms integration
- Import from CSV
- Manual entry
- API integration
- Email parsing

**Lead Scoring:**
```javascript
{
  criteria: [
    { field: "jobTitle", value: "C-Level", points: 20 },
    { field: "companySize", value: "100+", points: 15 },
    { field: "industry", value: "Technology", points: 10 },
    { field: "engagement", value: "Visited pricing page", points: 25 }
  ],
  
  totalScore: 70,
  grade: "A|B|C|D" // based on score ranges
}
```

**Lead Qualification:**
- BANT framework (Budget, Authority, Need, Timeline)
- Custom qualification criteria
- Auto-convert to opportunity when qualified

**Lead Assignment:**
- Round-robin distribution
- Territory-based assignment
- Lead pool for unassigned leads

#### Customer 360 View

**Unified Interface:**
- Contact information
- Communication history (all calls, emails, meetings)
- Deal history
- Order history
- Support tickets (if support module exists)
- Files and documents
- Notes and comments
- Activity timeline

### 3.6.3 Sales Analytics

**Reports:**
- **Sales Forecast:** Projected revenue by close date
- **Pipeline Report:** Deals by stage, value, probability
- **Win/Loss Analysis:** Why deals won or lost
- **Sales by Rep:** Individual performance
- **Lead Conversion Rate:** Lead → Opportunity → Customer
- **Sales Cycle Length:** Average time to close
- **Activity Report:** Calls, emails, meetings logged

**Dashboards:**
- Revenue YTD vs. target
- Pipeline value by stage
- Top deals closing this month
- Leaderboard (top sales reps)

## 3.7 Invoice & Billing Management

### 3.7.1 Overview

**Purpose:** Create, send, and track invoices with automated billing and payment processing.

**Target Users:** Service businesses, B2B (65% of enterprise users)

**Tier:** 🔒 **PREMIUM** ($55/month base + $1.50/user)

**Key Features:**
- Professional invoice creation
- Recurring billing
- Online payment acceptance
- Payment reminders
- Late fees
- Multi-currency
- Integration with accounting

**Invoice Schema:**
```javascript
{
  id: "uuid",
  invoiceNumber: "INV-2026-00123",
  
  customer: "customerId",
  
  invoiceDate: "2026-01-19",
  dueDate: "2026-02-18", // Net 30
  
  lineItems: [
    {
      description: "Website Development",
      quantity: 40,
      unitPrice: 75.00,
      amount: 3000.00,
      taxable: true
    }
  ],
  
  subtotal: 3000.00,
  taxRate: 0.08,
  taxAmount: 240.00,
  discount: 0,
  total: 3240.00,
  
  currency: "USD",
  
  paymentTerms: "net_30",
  
  status: "draft|sent|viewed|partial|paid|overdue|cancelled",
  
  paymentsMade: [
    {
      date: "2026-01-25",
      amount: 1240.00,
      method: "credit_card",
      reference: "ch_abc123"
    }
  ],
  
  amountPaid: 1240.00,
  amountDue: 2000.00,
  
  sentDate: "2026-01-19",
  viewedDate: "2026-01-20",
  paidDate: null,
  
  reminders: [
    { sentDate: "2026-02-05", type: "upcoming" },
    { sentDate: "2026-02-19", type: "overdue" }
  ],
  
  linkedOrder: "orderId",
  linkedProject: "projectId",
  
  notes: "Payment due within 30 days",
  terms: "Standard payment terms apply",
  
  attachments: ["contract.pdf"]
}
```

**Features:**
- Invoice templates (customizable)
- Logo and branding
- PDF generation
- Email delivery
- Online payment portal
- Partial payments
- Recurring invoices (subscriptions)
- Credit notes/refunds
- Payment reminders (automatic)
- Late fees (automatic or manual)

---

## 3.8 Team Communication Hub

### 3.8.1 Overview

**Purpose:** Centralized team communication with channels, direct messaging, and integrations.

**Target Users:** All enterprise users (95% adoption)

**Tier:** **FREE** (Core Feature, advanced features premium)

**Key Features:**
- Channels and direct messages
- File sharing
- Voice/video calls (🔒 Premium)
- Screen sharing
- Threaded conversations
- @mentions and notifications
- Search and archives
- Integration with other modules

**Channel Structure:**
```javascript
{
  id: "uuid",
  name: "general",
  displayName: "#general",
  
  type: "public|private|direct_message",
  
  description: "General company announcements",
  
  members: ["userId1", "userId2"],
  
  createdBy: "userId",
  createdDate: "2026-01-01",
  
  // Settings
  archived: false,
  notifications: "all|mentions|nothing",
  
  // Related
  project: "projectId", // optional project channel
  
  pinnedMessages: ["messageId1"]
}
```

**Features:**
- Emoji reactions
- Message editing and deletion
- Code snippets
- Polls
- Reminders
- Status updates (available, away, in meeting)

## 3.9 Document Management System

### 3.9.1 Overview

**Purpose:** Centralized document storage, organization, version control, and collaboration.

**Target Users:** All enterprise users (75% adoption)

**Tier:** 🔒 **PREMIUM** ($50/month base + 100GB storage)

**Key Features:**
- Folder hierarchy
- Version control
- Access permissions
- Document approval workflows
- Full-text search
- Document templates
- E-signatures (🔒 Premium Plus)
- Audit trail

**Document Schema:**
```javascript
{
  id: "uuid",
  name: "Client Proposal.docx",
  path: "/projects/website-redesign/proposals/",
  
  type: "file|folder",
  mimeType: "application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document",
  size: 524288, // bytes
  
  version: 3,
  versions: [
    { version: 1, uploadedBy: "userId1", uploadedDate: "2026-01-10", size: 450000 },
    { version: 2, uploadedBy: "userId1", uploadedDate: "2026-01-15", size: 500000 },
    { version: 3, uploadedBy: "userId2", uploadedDate: "2026-01-19", size: 524288 }
  ],
  
  uploadedBy: "userId",
  uploadedDate: "2026-01-19T14:30:00Z",
  
  lastModifiedBy: "userId2",
  lastModifiedDate: "2026-01-19T16:45:00Z",
  
  permissions: [
    { userId: "userId1", role: "owner" },
    { userId: "userId2", role: "editor" },
    { teamId: "teamId1", role: "viewer" }
  ],
  
  tags: ["proposal", "client", "2026"],
  
  relatedTo: {
    project: "projectId",
    customer: "customerId"
  },
  
  checkoutStatus: {
    checkedOut: true,
    checkedOutBy: "userId2",
    checkedOutDate: "2026-01-19T16:30:00Z"
  },
  
  approval: {
    required: true,
    status: "pending|approved|rejected",
    approvers: ["managerId"],
    approvedBy: null,
    approvedDate: null
  }
}
```

2. ✅ Team Communication - Core collaboration need

**Premium Features (Choose à la carte):**

5. 🔒 CRM - $65/month
6. 🔒 Order Management - $60/month
7. 🔒 Invoice & Billing - $55/month
8. 🔒 Inventory Management - $75/month
9. 🔒 Analytics Dashboard - $70/month
10. 🔒 Resource Planning - $60/month
11. 🔒 Document Management - $50/month
12. 🔒 Vendor Management - $45/month

**Bundle Options:**
- **Operations Bundle:** Inventory, Orders, Vendors - $150/month (save 25%)
- **Financial Bundle:** Finance, Invoicing, Analytics - $180/month (save 20%)
- **Complete Enterprise:** All 12 features - $400/month (save 45%)

**Pricing Notes:**
- Prices are base monthly fees
- Per-user fees apply ($1.50-$3/user depending on feature)
- Annual billing offers 20% discount
- Volume discounts for 50+ users

## 4.1 System Architecture Overview

### 4.1.1 High-Level Architecture

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                        CLIENT LAYER                              │
├──────────────┬──────────────────────┬───────────────────────────┤
│  Web App     │   iOS App (Swift)     │   Android App (Kotlin)   │
│  (Next.js)   │   Native UI           │   Material Design        │
│  React       │   SwiftUI             │   Jetpack Compose        │
└──────┬───────┴──────────┬────────────┴──────────┬───────────────┘
       │                  │                       │
       └──────────────────┼───────────────────────┘
                          │
                    ┌─────▼─────┐
                    │   CDN     │
                    │ (Cloudflare)│
                    └─────┬─────┘
                          │
       ┌──────────────────▼──────────────────┐
       │       API GATEWAY LAYER             │
       │  - Rate Limiting                    │
       │  - Authentication                   │
       │  - Request Routing                  │
       │  - Load Balancing                   │
       └──────────────┬──────────────────────┘
                      │
       ┌──────────────▼──────────────────────────────────┐
       │           BACKEND SERVICES LAYER                │
       ├────────────────────┬─────────────────────────────┤
       │  Core API          │  Feature Services           │
       │  (Express.js)      │  - Individual Features      │
       │  - User Management │  - Enterprise Features      │
       │  - Auth Service    │  - Analytics Service        │
       │  - Sync Service    │  - Notification Service     │
       └─────────┬──────────┴──────────┬──────────────────┘
                 │                     │
       ┌─────────▼─────────┐  ┌────────▼──────────────┐
       │   Primary DB      │  │   Services Layer      │
       │   (MongoDB)       │  │   - Redis Cache       │
       │   - User Data     │  │   - Message Queue     │
       │   - App Data      │  │   - File Storage (S3) │
       │   - Transactions  │  │   - Search (Elastic)  │
       └───────────────────┘  └───────────────────────┘
                 │
       ┌─────────▼─────────┐
       │  External APIs    │
       │  - Payment (Stripe)│
       │  - Email (SendGrid)│
       │  - SMS (Twilio)    │
       │  - Analytics       │
       └───────────────────┘
```

### 4.1.2 Architecture Principles

**1. Microservices-Oriented (Modular Monolith to Start)**
- Begin with modular monolith for faster development
- Clear service boundaries for future microservices split
- Feature modules are independently deployable units
- Shared core services (auth, sync, notifications)

**2. API-First Design**
- RESTful APIs with GraphQL for complex queries
- Comprehensive API documentation (OpenAPI/Swagger)
- Versioned APIs (v1, v2) for backward compatibility
- Consistent response formats and error handling

**3. Mobile-First, Cloud-Native**
- Responsive web design for all devices
- Native mobile apps for optimal UX
- Serverless functions for scaling
- Container-based deployment (Docker/Kubernetes)

**4. Real-Time & Offline-First**
- WebSocket connections for real-time updates
- Offline data persistence with sync queue
- Conflict resolution for concurrent edits
- Progressive Web App (PWA) capabilities

**5. Security by Design**
- Zero-trust architecture
- Encryption at rest and in transit
- Regular security audits
- OWASP Top 10 compliance
- SOC 2 Type II certification path

**6. Scalability & Performance**
- Horizontal scaling capabilities
- Caching strategies (Redis, CDN)
- Database indexing and optimization
- Lazy loading and code splitting
- Performance monitoring and optimization

### 4.1.3 Technology Stack Summary

| Layer | Technology | Purpose |
|-------|-----------|---------|
| **Frontend Web** | Next.js 14+ (App Router) | React framework with SSR/SSG |
| | TypeScript | Type safety |
| | Tailwind CSS | Utility-first styling |
| | Zustand/Redux | State management |
| | React Query | Server state management |
| **Mobile iOS** | Swift 5.9+ | Native iOS development |
| | SwiftUI | Declarative UI framework |
| | Combine | Reactive programming |
| | Core Data | Local persistence |
| **Mobile Android** | Kotlin 1.9+ | Native Android development |
| | Jetpack Compose | Modern UI toolkit |
| | Coroutines/Flow | Async programming |
| | Room | Local database |
| **Backend** | Node.js 20+ LTS | Runtime environment |
| | Express.js 4.x | Web framework |
| | TypeScript | Type safety |
| | Socket.IO | WebSocket communication |
| **Database** | MongoDB 7.0+ | Primary database |
| | Redis 7.x | Caching & sessions |
| | Elasticsearch 8.x | Full-text search |
| **Infrastructure** | Docker | Containerization |
| | Kubernetes | Container orchestration |
| | AWS/GCP | Cloud provider |
| | Terraform | Infrastructure as Code |
| **DevOps** | GitHub Actions | CI/CD pipeline |
| | Jest/Vitest | Testing |
| | Sentry | Error tracking |
| | Datadog | Monitoring & APM |

### 4.1.4 Deployment Architecture

```
Production Environment:

┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    AWS/GCP CLOUD                         │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                          │
│  ┌────────────────────────────────────────────┐        │
│  │  Region 1 (Primary - US-East)              │        │
│  │  ┌──────────────────────────────────────┐  │        │
│  │  │  Availability Zone A                 │  │        │
│  │  │  - Web Servers (Auto-scaling)        │  │        │
│  │  │  - API Servers (Auto-scaling)        │  │        │
│  │  │  - Redis Cluster (Master)            │  │        │
│  │  └──────────────────────────────────────┘  │        │
│  │  ┌──────────────────────────────────────┐  │        │
│  │  │  Availability Zone B                 │  │        │
│  │  │  - Web Servers (Auto-scaling)        │  │        │
│  │  │  - API Servers (Auto-scaling)        │  │        │
│  │  │  - Redis Cluster (Replica)           │  │        │
│  │  └──────────────────────────────────────┘  │        │
│  │  ┌──────────────────────────────────────┐  │        │
│  │  │  MongoDB Atlas Cluster               │  │        │
│  │  │  - Multi-AZ Replica Set              │  │        │
│  │  │  - Automated Backups                 │  │        │
│  │  └──────────────────────────────────────┘  │        │
│  └────────────────────────────────────────────┘        │
│                                                          │
│  ┌────────────────────────────────────────────┐        │
│  │  Region 2 (DR - US-West)                   │        │
│  │  - Hot Standby                             │        │
│  │  - Database Read Replicas                  │        │
│  │  - Disaster Recovery                       │        │
│  └────────────────────────────────────────────┘        │
│                                                          │
│  ┌────────────────────────────────────────────┐        │
│  │  Global Services                           │        │
│  │  - CloudFront CDN                          │        │
│  │  - S3 Object Storage                       │        │
│  │  - Route 53 DNS                            │        │
│  │  - CloudWatch Monitoring                   │        │
│  └────────────────────────────────────────────┘        │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**Environments:**
- **Development:** Local Docker Compose setup
- **Staging:** Mirrors production, smaller scale
- **Production:** Multi-region, auto-scaling, HA
- **Testing:** Isolated environment for QA

## 4.2 Monorepo Structure

### 4.2.1 Repository Organization

```
prms-monorepo/
├── apps/
│   ├── web/                      # Next.js web application
│   │   ├── src/
│   │   │   ├── app/              # Next.js 14 App Router
│   │   │   │   ├── (auth)/       # Auth route group
│   │   │   │   ├── (individual)/ # Individual mode routes
│   │   │   │   ├── (enterprise)/ # Enterprise mode routes
│   │   │   │   ├── api/          # API routes
│   │   │   │   └── layout.tsx
│   │   │   ├── components/       # React components
│   │   │   │   ├── ui/           # Base UI components
│   │   │   │   ├── features/     # Feature-specific components
│   │   │   │   └── layouts/      # Layout components
│   │   │   ├── lib/              # Utilities and helpers
│   │   │   ├── hooks/            # Custom React hooks
│   │   │   ├── store/            # State management (Zustand)
│   │   │   ├── styles/           # Global styles
│   │   │   └── types/            # TypeScript types
│   │   ├── public/               # Static assets
│   │   ├── next.config.js
│   │   ├── tailwind.config.js
│   │   └── package.json
│   │
│   ├── mobile-ios/               # Swift iOS application
│   │   ├── PrMS/
│   │   │   ├── App/              # App entry point
│   │   │   ├── Core/             # Core utilities
│   │   │   │   ├── Network/      # API client
│   │   │   │   ├── Storage/      # CoreData/UserDefaults
│   │   │   │   ├── Auth/         # Authentication
│   │   │   │   └── Sync/         # Offline sync
│   │   │   ├── Features/         # Feature modules
│   │   │   │   ├── Tasks/
│   │   │   │   ├── Calendar/
│   │   │   │   ├── Finance/
│   │   │   │   └── ...
│   │   │   ├── Shared/           # Shared components
│   │   │   │   ├── UI/           # SwiftUI components
│   │   │   │   ├── Models/       # Data models
```

### 4.2.2 Monorepo Tooling

**Build System: Turborepo**
```json
// turbo.json
{
  "pipeline": {
    "build": {
      "dependsOn": ["^build"],
      "outputs": [".next/**", "dist/**", "build/**"]
    },
    "test": {
      "dependsOn": ["^build"],
      "outputs": ["coverage/**"]
    },
    "lint": {
      "outputs": []
    },
    "dev": {
      "cache": false,
      "persistent": true
    }
  }
}
```

**Package Manager: pnpm**
- Efficient disk space usage
- Faster installations
- Strict dependency resolution
- Workspace protocol support

**Advantages:**
- Code sharing across apps (types, utils, UI components)
- Unified dependency management
- Consistent tooling and linting
- Atomic commits across all apps
- Simplified CI/CD

---

### 4.3.2 State Management Strategy

**Client State: Zustand**
```typescript
// store/userStore.ts
import { create } from 'zustand'
import { persist } from 'zustand/middleware'

interface UserState {
  user: User | null
  mode: 'individual' | 'enterprise'
  setUser: (user: User) => void
  setMode: (mode: 'individual' | 'enterprise') => void
  logout: () => void
}

export const useUserStore = create<UserState>()(
  persist(
    (set) => ({
      user: null,
      mode: 'individual',
      setUser: (user) => set({ user }),
      setMode: (mode) => set({ mode }),
      logout: () => set({ user: null }),
    }),
    {
      name: 'user-storage',
    }
  )
)
```

**Server State: React Query**
```typescript
// hooks/useTasks.ts
import { useQuery, useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query'

export function useTasks() {
  return useQuery({
    queryKey: ['tasks'],
    queryFn: async () => {
      const res = await fetch('/api/tasks')
      return res.json()
    },
  })
}

export function useCreateTask() {
  const queryClient = useQueryClient()
  
  return useMutation({
    mutationFn: async (task: NewTask) => {
      const res = await fetch('/api/tasks', {
        method: 'POST',
        body: JSON.stringify(task),
      })
      return res.json()
    },
    onSuccess: () => {
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['tasks'] })
    },
  })
}
```

### 4.3.3 Component Architecture

**Component Hierarchy:**
```
Pages (Route Components)
  └─── Layouts (Shared structure)
        └─── Features (Business logic components)
              └─── UI Components (Reusable, presentational)
```

**Example Feature Component:**
```typescript
// components/features/TaskList/TaskList.tsx
'use client'

import { useTasks } from '@/hooks/useTasks'
import { TaskItem } from './TaskItem'
import { Button, Spinner } from '@/components/ui'

export function TaskList() {
  const { data: tasks, isLoading, error } = useTasks()
  const createTask = useCreateTask()

  if (isLoading) return <Spinner />
  if (error) return <ErrorMessage error={error} />

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
        <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold">Tasks</h2>
        <Button onClick={() => createTask.mutate({ title: 'New Task' })}>
          Add Task
        </Button>
      </div>
      
      <div className="space-y-2">
        {tasks?.map(task => (
          <TaskItem key={task.id} task={task} />
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}
```

### 4.3.5 Offline Support (PWA)

**Service Worker:**

```typescript
// next.config.js with next-pwa

  dest: 'public',

  skipWaiting: true,
```

**Offline Data Sync:**
```typescript
// lib/offlineSync.ts
import { openDB } from 'idb'

const db = await openDB('prms-offline', 1, {
  upgrade(db) {
    db.createObjectStore('pendingActions')
  },
})

export async function queueAction(action: Action) {
  await db.add('pendingActions', action)
}

export async function syncPendingActions() {
  const actions = await db.getAll('pendingActions')
  for (const action of actions) {
    await processAction(action)
    await db.delete('pendingActions', action.id)
  }
}
```

## 4.4 Mobile Architecture (Kotlin & Swift)

### 4.4.1 iOS Architecture (Swift)

**MVVM + Clean Architecture:**
```
PrMS iOS App
├── Presentation Layer
│   ├── ViewModels (ObservableObject)
│   └── Views (SwiftUI)
│
├── Domain Layer
│   ├── Use Cases
│   ├── Entities
│   └── Repository Protocols
│
└── Data Layer
    ├── Repository Implementations
    ├── Network (URLSession/Alamofire)
    ├── Local Storage (CoreData)
    └── Cache (UserDefaults)
```

**Example Feature Module:**
```swift
// Features/Tasks/Domain/TaskRepository.swift
protocol TaskRepository {
    func getTasks() async throws -> [Task]
    func createTask(_ task: Task) async throws -> Task
    func updateTask(_ task: Task) async throws
    func deleteTask(id: String) async throws
}

// Features/Tasks/Data/TaskRepositoryImpl.swift
class TaskRepositoryImpl: TaskRepository {
    private let apiClient: APIClient
    private let localStorage: LocalStorage
    
    func getTasks() async throws -> [Task] {
        do {
            let tasks = try await apiClient.get("/tasks")
            await localStorage.save(tasks)
            return tasks
        } catch {
            // Return cached data if offline
            return await localStorage.getTasks()
        }
    }
}

// Features/Tasks/Presentation/TaskListViewModel.swift
@MainActor
class TaskListViewModel: ObservableObject {
    @Published var tasks: [Task] = []
    @Published var isLoading = false
    @Published var error: Error?
    
    private let repository: TaskRepository
    
    init(repository: TaskRepository) {
        self.repository = repository
    }
    
    func loadTasks() async {
        isLoading = true
        do {
            tasks = try await repository.getTasks()
        } catch {
            self.error = error
        }
        isLoading = false
    }
}

// Features/Tasks/Presentation/TaskListView.swift
struct TaskListView: View {
    @StateObject var viewModel: TaskListViewModel
    
    var body: some View {
        List(viewModel.tasks) { task in
            TaskRow(task: task)
        }
        .task {
            await viewModel.loadTasks()
        }
    }
}
```

**Networking Layer:**
```swift
// Core/Network/APIClient.swift
class APIClient {
    private let baseURL = "https://api.prms.app/v1"
    private let session: URLSession
    
    func get<T: Decodable>(_ endpoint: String) async throws -> T {
        let url = URL(string: baseURL + endpoint)!
        var request = URLRequest(url: url)
        request.addValue("Bearer \(authToken)", forHTTPHeaderField: "Authorization")
        
        let (data, response) = try await session.data(for: request)
        
        guard let httpResponse = response as? HTTPURLResponse,
              (200...299).contains(httpResponse.statusCode) else {
            throw APIError.invalidResponse
        }
        
        return try JSONDecoder().decode(T.self, from: data)
    }
}
```

**Offline Sync:**
```swift
// Core/Sync/SyncManager.swift
actor SyncManager {
    private let coreData: CoreDataStack
    private let apiClient: APIClient
    
    func sync() async {
        // 1. Upload pending changes
        let pending = await coreData.getPendingChanges()
        for change in pending {
            do {
                try await uploadChange(change)
                await coreData.markAsSynced(change)
            } catch {
                print("Sync failed: \(error)")
            }
        }
        
        // 2. Download remote changes
        let lastSync = await coreData.getLastSyncTimestamp()
        let changes = try? await apiClient.get("/sync?since=\(lastSync)")
        await coreData.applyRemoteChanges(changes)
    }
}
```

### 4.4.2 Android Architecture (Kotlin)

**MVVM + Clean Architecture:**
```kotlin
// features/tasks/domain/repository/TaskRepository.kt
interface TaskRepository {
    suspend fun getTasks(): Flow<Result<List<Task>>>
    suspend fun createTask(task: Task): Result<Task>
    suspend fun updateTask(task: Task): Result<Unit>
    suspend fun deleteTask(id: String): Result<Unit>
}

// features/tasks/data/repository/TaskRepositoryImpl.kt
class TaskRepositoryImpl @Inject constructor(
    private val apiService: ApiService,
    private val taskDao: TaskDao,
    private val networkMonitor: NetworkMonitor
) : TaskRepository {
    
    override suspend fun getTasks(): Flow<Result<List<Task>>> = flow {
        // Try local cache first
        emit(Result.Loading)
        
        val cachedTasks = taskDao.getAllTasks().first()
        if (cachedTasks.isNotEmpty()) {
            emit(Result.Success(cachedTasks))
        }
        
        // Fetch from network if online
        if (networkMonitor.isOnline.first()) {
            try {
                val remoteTasks = apiService.getTasks()
                taskDao.insertAll(remoteTasks)
                emit(Result.Success(remoteTasks))
            } catch (e: Exception) {
                emit(Result.Error(e))
            }
        }
    }
}

// features/tasks/presentation/TaskListViewModel.kt
@HiltViewModel
class TaskListViewModel @Inject constructor(
    private val repository: TaskRepository
) : ViewModel() {
    
    private val _uiState = MutableStateFlow<TaskListUiState>(TaskListUiState.Loading)
    val uiState: StateFlow<TaskListUiState> = _uiState.asStateFlow()
    
    init {
        loadTasks()
    }
    
    private fun loadTasks() {
        viewModelScope.launch {
            repository.getTasks().collect { result ->
                _uiState.value = when (result) {
                    is Result.Loading -> TaskListUiState.Loading
                    is Result.Success -> TaskListUiState.Success(result.data)
                    is Result.Error -> TaskListUiState.Error(result.exception)
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

// features/tasks/presentation/TaskListScreen.kt
@Composable
fun TaskListScreen(
    viewModel: TaskListViewModel = hiltViewModel()
) {
    val uiState by viewModel.uiState.collectAsState()
    
    when (val state = uiState) {
        is TaskListUiState.Loading -> LoadingIndicator()
        is TaskListUiState.Success -> {
            LazyColumn {
                items(state.tasks) { task ->
                    TaskItem(task = task)
                }
            }
        }
        is TaskListUiState.Error -> ErrorMessage(state.exception)
    }
}
```

**Local Database (Room):**
```kotlin
// core/database/entities/TaskEntity.kt
@Entity(tableName = "tasks")
data class TaskEntity(
    @PrimaryKey val id: String,
    val title: String,
    val description: String?,
    val status: String,
    val dueDate: Long?,
    val createdAt: Long,
    val updatedAt: Long,
    @ColumnInfo(name = "sync_status") 
    val syncStatus: SyncStatus
)

// core/database/dao/TaskDao.kt
@Dao
interface TaskDao {
    @Query("SELECT * FROM tasks WHERE sync_status != 'DELETED'")
    fun getAllTasks(): Flow<List<TaskEntity>>
    
    @Insert(onConflict = OnConflictStrategy.REPLACE)
    suspend fun insertAll(tasks: List<TaskEntity>)
    
    @Update
    suspend fun update(task: TaskEntity)
    
    @Query("DELETE FROM tasks WHERE id = :taskId")
    suspend fun delete(taskId: String)
    
    @Query("SELECT * FROM tasks WHERE sync_status = 'PENDING'")
    suspend fun getPendingSync(): List<TaskEntity>
}
```

**Dependency Injection (Hilt):**
```kotlin
// di/AppModule.kt
@Module
@InstallIn(SingletonComponent::class)
object AppModule {
    
    @Provides
    @Singleton
    fun provideRetrofit(): Retrofit {
        return Retrofit.Builder()
            .baseUrl("https://api.prms.app/v1/")
            .addConverterFactory(GsonConverterFactory.create())
            .build()
    }
    
    @Provides
    @Singleton
    fun provideApiService(retrofit: Retrofit): ApiService {
        return retrofit.create(ApiService::class.java)
    }
    
    @Provides
    @Singleton
    fun provideDatabase(@ApplicationContext context: Context): PrmsDatabase {
        return Room.databaseBuilder(
            context,
            PrmsDatabase::class.java,
            "prms_database"
        ).build()
    }
}
```

### 4.4.3 Mobile Offline Sync Strategy

**Sync Protocol:**
```
1. Queue local changes (CRUD operations)
2. Periodically sync when online:
   a. Upload pending local changes
   b. Download remote changes since last sync
   c. Resolve conflicts (last-write-wins or manual)
3. Update local database
4. Notify UI of changes
```

**Conflict Resolution:**
```kotlin
data class SyncConflict(
    val localVersion: Entity,
    val remoteVersion: Entity,
    val timestamp: Long
)

sealed class ConflictResolution {
    object UseLocal : ConflictResolution()
    object UseRemote : ConflictResolution()
    data class Merge(val merged: Entity) : ConflictResolution()
}
```

## 4.5 Backend Architecture (Express.js)

### 4.5.1 Application Structure

**Layered Architecture:**
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────┐
│         Routes Layer                │  ← HTTP endpoints
├─────────────────────────────────────┤
│       Controllers Layer             │  ← Request handling
├─────────────────────────────────────┤
│        Services Layer               │  ← Business logic
├─────────────────────────────────────┤
│      Repositories Layer             │  ← Data access
├─────────────────────────────────────┤
│         Models Layer                │  ← Database schemas
└─────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**Example Implementation:**
```typescript
// routes/tasks.routes.ts
import { Router } from 'express'
import { TaskController } from '../controllers/task.controller'
import { authenticate } from '../middleware/auth'
import { validate } from '../middleware/validation'
import { createTaskSchema } from '../validators/task.validator'

const router = Router()
const controller = new TaskController()

router.use(authenticate)

router.get('/', controller.getTasks)
router.post('/', validate(createTaskSchema), controller.createTask)
router.put('/:id', controller.updateTask)
router.delete('/:id', controller.deleteTask)

export default router

// controllers/task.controller.ts
export class TaskController {
  private taskService = new TaskService()

  getTasks = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
    try {
      const tasks = await this.taskService.getUserTasks(req.user.id)
      res.json({ success: true, data: tasks })
    } catch (error) {
      next(error)
    }
  }

  createTask = async (req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => {
    try {
      const task = await this.taskService.createTask({
        ...req.body,
        userId: req.user.id
      })
      res.status(201).json({ success: true, data: task })
    } catch (error) {
      next(error)
    }
  }
}

// services/task.service.ts
export class TaskService {
  private taskRepository = new TaskRepository()
  private notificationService = new NotificationService()
  private syncService = new SyncService()

  async getUserTasks(userId: string): Promise<Task[]> {
    return this.taskRepository.findByUserId(userId)
  }

  async createTask(data: CreateTaskDTO): Promise<Task> {
    // Business logic
    const task = await this.taskRepository.create(data)
    
    // Side effects
    await this.notificationService.sendTaskCreated(task)
    await this.syncService.broadcastUpdate(data.userId, 'task_created', task)
    
    return task
  }
}

// repositories/task.repository.ts
export class TaskRepository {
  private model = TaskModel

  async findByUserId(userId: string): Promise<Task[]> {
    return this.model.find({ userId, deleted: false }).sort({ createdAt: -1 })
  }

  async create(data: CreateTaskDTO): Promise<Task> {
    const task = new this.model(data)
    return task.save()
  }
}
```

### 4.5.2 API Design Patterns

**RESTful API Structure:**
```
/api/v1
├── /auth
│   ├── POST /register
│   ├── POST /login
│   ├── POST /logout
│   ├── POST /refresh
│   └── POST /forgot-password
│
├── /users
│   ├── GET /:id
│   ├── PUT /:id
│   └── DELETE /:id
│
├── /individual
│   ├── /tasks
│   │   ├── GET /
│   │   ├── POST /
│   │   ├── GET /:id
│   │   ├── PUT /:id
│   │   └── DELETE /:id
│   ├── /calendar
│   ├── /finance
│   └── ...
│
└── /enterprise
    ├── /projects
    ├── /inventory
    ├── /orders
    └── ...
```

**Response Format:**
```typescript
interface ApiResponse<T> {
  success: boolean
  data?: T
  error?: {
    code: string
    message: string
    details?: any
  }
  meta?: {
    total?: number
    page?: number
    limit?: number
  }
}

// Success response
{
  "success": true,
  "data": [...],
  "meta": {
    "total": 100,
    "page": 1,
    "limit": 20
  }
}

// Error response
{
  "success": false,
  "error": {
    "code": "TASK_NOT_FOUND",
    "message": "Task with ID 123 not found"
  }
}
```

### 4.5.3 Middleware Stack

```typescript
// app.ts
import express from 'express'
import helmet from 'helmet'
import cors from 'cors'
import compression from 'compression'
import rateLimit from 'express-rate-limit'

const app = express()

// Security
app.use(helmet())
app.use(cors({
  origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS?.split(','),
  credentials: true
}))

// Body parsing
app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }))
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }))

// Compression
app.use(compression())

// Rate limiting
const limiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
  max: 100, // limit each IP to 100 requests per windowMs
  message: 'Too many requests from this IP'
})
app.use('/api/', limiter)

// Logging
app.use(morgan('combined'))

// Custom middleware
app.use(requestId)
app.use(authenticate)

// Routes
app.use('/api/v1', routes)

// Error handling
app.use(notFoundHandler)
app.use(errorHandler)
```

### 4.5.4 Real-Time Communication

**WebSocket Server:**
```typescript
// server.ts
import { Server } from 'socket.io'
import { createServer } from 'http'

const httpServer = createServer(app)
const io = new Server(httpServer, {
  cors: {
    origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS?.split(','),
    credentials: true
  }
})

// Authentication middleware
io.use(async (socket, next) => {
  const token = socket.handshake.auth.token
  try {
    const user = await verifyToken(token)
    socket.data.user = user
    next()
  } catch (err) {
    next(new Error('Authentication failed'))
  }
})

// Connection handling
io.on('connection', (socket) => {
  const userId = socket.data.user.id
  
  // Join user's personal room
  socket.join(`user:${userId}`)
  
  // Join enterprise rooms if applicable
  if (socket.data.user.enterpriseId) {
    socket.join(`enterprise:${socket.data.user.enterpriseId}`)
  }
  
  // Event handlers
  socket.on('task:update', async (data) => {
    const task = await taskService.updateTask(data)
    socket.to(`user:${userId}`).emit('task:updated', task)
  })
  
  socket.on('disconnect', () => {
    console.log('User disconnected:', userId)
  })
})

// Broadcasting updates from services
export function broadcastToUser(userId: string, event: string, data: any) {
  io.to(`user:${userId}`).emit(event, data)
}
```

### 4.5.5 Background Jobs

**Job Queue (Bull):**
```typescript
// queues/emailQueue.ts
import Queue from 'bull'
import { sendEmail } from '../services/email.service'

export const emailQueue = new Queue('email', {
  redis: {
    host: process.env.REDIS_HOST,
    port: Number(process.env.REDIS_PORT)
  }
})

emailQueue.process(async (job) => {
  const { to, subject, body } = job.data
  await sendEmail(to, subject, body)
})

// Usage in service
await emailQueue.add({
  to: 'user@example.com',
  subject: 'Welcome to PrMS',
  body: '...'
}, {
  attempts: 3,
  backoff: {
    type: 'exponential',
    delay: 2000
  }
})
```

**Scheduled Jobs (node-cron):**
```typescript
// jobs/scheduledJobs.ts
import cron from 'node-cron'

// Daily reminder notifications - 8 AM
cron.schedule('0 8 * * *', async () => {
  await sendDailyReminders()
})

// Weekly reports - Sunday 9 PM
cron.schedule('0 21 * * 0', async () => {
  await generateWeeklyReports()
})

// Cleanup old data - Daily 2 AM
cron.schedule('0 2 * * *', async () => {
  await cleanupOldData()
})
```
