## 8.6 Unit Economics

### 8.6.1 Individual User Economics

**Average Revenue Per User (ARPU):**
```
Paid Users: 15% of total
Average Features: 2.5 per paid user
Average Price: $5/feature/month
ARPU (paid users): $12.50/month
ARPU (all users): $1.88/month
```

**Lifetime Value (LTV) Calculation:**
```
Average Subscription Length: 24 months
Monthly Revenue: $12.50
Annual Revenue: $150
LTV = $12.50 × 24 = $300

Conservative (12 months): $150
Optimistic (36 months): $450
```

**Customer Acquisition Cost (CAC):**
```
Blended CAC: $15
LTV/CAC Ratio: 20:1 (excellent)
Payback Period: 1.2 months
```

**Contribution Margin:**
```
Monthly Revenue: $12.50
Cost to Serve: $0.50 (infrastructure, support)
Contribution Margin: $12.00
Contribution Margin %: 96%
```

### 8.6.2 Enterprise Customer Economics

**Average Revenue Per Account (ARPA):**
```
Starter Plan: $199/month
Professional Plan: $499/month
Enterprise Plan: $999/month
Weighted Average: $400/month
```

**Lifetime Value (LTV):**
```
Average Contract Length: 36 months
Monthly Revenue: $400
LTV = $400 × 36 = $14,400

Conservative (24 months): $9,600
Optimistic (48 months): $19,200
```

**Customer Acquisition Cost (CAC):**
```
Sales & Marketing: $2,000
LTV/CAC Ratio: 7.2:1 (healthy)
Payback Period: 5 months
```

**Annual Contract Value (ACV):**
```
Starter: $2,388
Professional: $5,988
Enterprise: $11,988
Average ACV: $4,800
```

### 8.6.3 Cohort Analysis

**Month 1 Cohort (1,000 users):**

| Month | Active Users | Retention % | Paid Users | Conversion % | MRR | Cumulative Revenue |
|-------|--------------|-------------|------------|--------------|-----|-------------------|
| 1 | 1,000 | 100% | 150 | 15% | $1,875 | $1,875 |
| 2 | 600 | 60% | 120 | 20% | $1,500 | $3,375 |
| 3 | 450 | 45% | 110 | 24% | $1,375 | $4,750 |
| 6 | 350 | 35% | 105 | 30% | $1,313 | $12,638 |
| 12 | 250 | 25% | 100 | 40% | $1,250 | $27,388 |

**Cohort LTV:** $27.39 per user

### 8.6.4 Key Metrics Targets

**Growth Metrics:**
- Monthly User Growth: 20% MoM (Year 1)
- Paid Conversion Rate: 15%
- Viral Coefficient: 0.3
- Monthly Active Users (MAU): 40% of total users

**Revenue Metrics:**
- MRR Growth: 25% MoM
- ARR: $1.6M (Year 1), $5.6M (Year 2), $15.5M (Year 3)
- Net Revenue Retention: 110%
- Gross Revenue Retention: 85%

**Efficiency Metrics:**
- CAC: $15 (individual), $2,000 (enterprise)
- LTV: $300 (individual), $14,400 (enterprise)
- LTV/CAC: 20:1 (individual), 7.2:1 (enterprise)
- Gross Margin: 90%
- Rule of 40: 50%+ (Growth % + Profit %)

**Engagement Metrics:**
- Daily Active Users (DAU): 25% of MAU
- Feature Adoption: 70% use 2+ features
- Weekly Engagement: 3+ sessions/week
- NPS Score: 50+

---

## 8.7 Competitive Analysis

### 8.7.1 Competitive Landscape

**Direct Competitors:**

**1. Notion**
- **Pricing:** Free, Personal Pro $10/month, Team $15/user/month
- **Strengths:** Flexibility, databases, collaboration
- **Weaknesses:** Steep learning curve, performance issues
- **Our Advantage:** Simpler UI, better mobile, à la carte pricing

**2. ClickUp**
- **Pricing:** Free, Unlimited $7/user/month, Business $12/user/month
- **Strengths:** Feature-rich, customization, views
- **Weaknesses:** Complexity, overwhelming, expensive
- **Our Advantage:** Simpler, pay-per-feature, better UX

**3. Asana**
- **Pricing:** Free, Premium $10.99/user/month, Business $24.99/user/month
- **Strengths:** Project management, team collaboration
- **Weaknesses:** Limited free tier, expensive, focused on tasks
- **Our Advantage:** More features, better pricing, individual focus

**4. Monday.com**
- **Pricing:** Individual $8/seat/month, Basic $24/user/month, Standard $30/user/month
- **Strengths:** Visual, customizable, integrations
- **Weaknesses:** Very expensive, overkill for individuals
- **Our Advantage:** 70% cheaper, individual features, simpler

**5. Todoist**
- **Pricing:** Free, Pro $4/month, Business $6/user/month
- **Strengths:** Simple, fast, reliable
- **Weaknesses:** Limited features, basic, task-only
- **Our Advantage:** More features, same price point, all-in-one

### 8.7.2 Competitive Positioning

**Positioning Matrix:**
```
                    High Price
                        │
        Monday.com      │      Asana
                        │
    ClickUp             │
Complexity ─────────────┼───────────── Simplicity
                        │
        Notion          │      PrMS
                        │    Todoist
                    Low Price
```

**Our Unique Position:**
- **Simplicity + Affordability + Modularity**
- Better than Notion: Easier to use, better mobile
- Better than ClickUp: Less complex, more affordable
- Better than Monday.com: 70% cheaper
- Better than Todoist: More features, same price

### 8.7.3 Competitive Advantages

**1. À La Carte Pricing:**
- Only competitor: None (all require full subscriptions)
- Advantage: Pay only for what you use
- Market opportunity: $2B+ (underserved)

**2. Dual Market Focus:**
- Individual + Enterprise in one platform
- Seamless transition as users grow
- Network effects between segments

**3. Better Mobile Experience:**
- Offline-first architecture
- Native iOS/Android apps
- Fast, reliable sync

**4. Fair Pricing:**
- 30-50% cheaper than competitors
- Transparent pricing
- No hidden fees
- Annual discounts

**5. Superior UX:**
- Intuitive design
- Less clutter
- Faster onboarding
- Better accessibility

### 8.7.4 Market Opportunity

**Total Addressable Market (TAM):**
```
Individual Productivity Software:  $8B
Enterprise Productivity Software:  $12B
Total TAM:                         $20B
```

**Serviceable Addressable Market (SAM):**
```
English-speaking markets:          $12B
Our target segments:               $8B
```

**Serviceable Obtainable Market (SOM):**
```
Year 1: 0.02% of SAM = $1.6M
Year 3: 0.19% of SAM = $15.5M
Year 5: 1% of SAM = $80M (projected)
```

**Market Share Targets:**
- Year 1: Capture 50,000 users (0.01% of market)
- Year 3: Capture 450,000 users (0.1% of market)
- Year 5: Capture 2M users (0.5% of market)

### 8.7.5 Barriers to Entry

**Our Moats:**

**1. Network Effects:**
- Team collaboration drives virality
- User-generated templates
- Community knowledge base

**2. Data Lock-in:**
- Years of user data and history
- Switching cost increases over time
- Export/migration friction

**3. Brand & Trust:**
- First-mover in à la carte model
- User reviews and testimonials
- Industry recognition

**4. Technology:**
- Proprietary sync algorithm
- Offline-first architecture
- AI/ML models (future)

**5. Economies of Scale:**
- Lower cost per user over time
- Better unit economics
- Negotiating power with vendors

## 9.1 Development Phases

### 9.1.1 Phase Overview

**Phase 0: Foundation (Months 1-2)**
- Infrastructure setup
- CI/CD pipeline
- Design system
- Core architecture
- Team onboarding

**Phase 1: MVP (Months 3-5)**
- 3 free individual features
- Authentication & user management
- Basic mobile apps
- Payment integration
- Core infrastructure

**Phase 2: Premium Features (Months 6-12)**
- Release 2 premium features/month
- Enhanced analytics
- Integration ecosystem
- Performance optimization
- User feedback iteration

**Phase 3: Enterprise Launch (Months 13-18)**
- Enterprise authentication (SSO)
- Team collaboration features
- Advanced permissions
- Admin dashboard
- Enterprise integrations

**Phase 4: Scale & Optimize (Months 19-24)**
- AI-powered features
- Advanced analytics
- White-label options
- Global expansion
- Performance at scale

### 9.1.2 Development Methodology

**Framework:** Agile/Scrum

**Sprint Structure:**
- Sprint Length: 2 weeks
- Planning: Monday (4 hours)
- Daily Standups: 15 minutes
- Sprint Review: Last Friday (2 hours)
- Retrospective: Last Friday (1 hour)

**Release Cadence:**
- Web: Weekly releases (Friday)
- Mobile: Bi-weekly releases (App Store review time)
- Hotfixes: As needed (within 4 hours for critical)

**Quality Gates:**
- Code review required
- 80%+ test coverage
- No critical bugs
- Performance benchmarks met
- Accessibility audit passed

---

## 9.2 MVP Strategy

### 9.2.1 MVP Scope

**Core Philosophy:** 
- Solve ONE problem exceptionally well
- Get to market fast (3 months)
- Learn from real users
- Iterate based on feedback

**MVP Features:**

**1. Task Management (FREE)**
```
Must Have:
✓ Create/edit/delete tasks
✓ Due dates and priorities
✓ Simple organization (tags)
✓ Mobile apps (iOS/Android)
✓ Web app
✓ Real-time sync

Nice to Have (post-MVP):
○ Subtasks
○ Recurring tasks
○ File attachments
○ Advanced filters
```

**2. Event Tracker & Calendar (FREE)**
```
Must Have:
✓ Create/edit/delete events
✓ Calendar views (month, week, day)
✓ Reminders
✓ Google Calendar sync
✓ Mobile & web

Nice to Have (post-MVP):
○ Recurring events
○ Multiple calendars
○ Calendar sharing
○ Outlook integration
```

**3. Note Taking (FREE)**
```
Must Have:
✓ Create/edit/delete notes
✓ Rich text editor
✓ Organization (notebooks)
✓ Search
✓ Mobile & web

Nice to Have (post-MVP):
○ Markdown support
○ Code highlighting
○ Templates
○ Version history
```

**Supporting Systems:**
```
Authentication:
✓ Email/password signup
✓ Google OAuth
✓ Password reset
✓ Email verification

Payment System:
✓ Stripe integration
✓ Subscription management
✓ Payment methods
✓ Billing portal

User Management:
✓ Profile settings
✓ Preferences
✓ Account deletion
✓ Data export
```

### 9.2.2 MVP Success Criteria

**Launch Criteria:**
- All 3 free features functional
- Mobile apps in app stores
- Payment system live
- No critical bugs
- Core user flows tested
- Basic analytics tracking

**Success Metrics (First 3 Months):**
- 10,000 signups
- 30% activation rate (3+ sessions)
- 10% conversion to paid (any premium feature)
- <5% churn rate
- NPS score: 40+
- Average session: 15+ minutes

### 9.2.3 MVP Timeline

**Month 1-2: Foundation**
```
Week 1-2: Infrastructure
- Set up monorepo
- Configure CI/CD
- Database setup (MongoDB Atlas)
- Authentication service
- Deployment pipeline

Week 3-4: Core Backend
- User API
- Task API
- Calendar API
- Notes API
- WebSocket server

Week 5-6: Frontend Foundation
- Design system implementation
- Component library
- State management
- API client
- Routing

Week 7-8: Mobile Foundation
- iOS project setup
- Android project setup
- Shared business logic
- Offline storage
- Sync service
```

**Month 3-4: Feature Development**
```
Week 9-10: Tasks Feature
- Backend complete
- Web UI complete
- iOS app complete
- Android app complete
- Testing

Week 11-12: Calendar Feature
- Backend complete
- Web UI complete
- Mobile apps complete
- Google Calendar integration
- Testing

Week 13-14: Notes Feature
- Backend complete
- Rich text editor
- Mobile apps complete
- Search functionality
- Testing

Week 15-16: Integration & Polish
- End-to-end testing
- Bug fixes
- Performance optimization
- UI polish
- Documentation
```

**Month 5: Beta & Launch**
```
Week 17-18: Private Beta
- Invite 100 beta users
- Monitor usage
- Fix critical bugs
- Gather feedback
- Iterate

Week 19-20: Public Launch
- Final QA
- App store submissions
- Marketing launch
- Monitor metrics
- Support setup
```

### 9.5.3 Technical Debt Management

**Debt Allocation:**
- 20% of each sprint for technical debt
- Dedicated "Tech Health" sprint every 6 sprints
- No new features in tech health sprint

**Debt Categories:**

**Critical (Fix Immediately):**
- Security vulnerabilities
- Data corruption risks
- Performance degradation >50%
- Accessibility blockers

**High (Fix in 2 sprints):**
- Performance issues
- Flaky tests
- Poor error handling
- Missing monitoring

**Medium (Fix in 4 sprints):**
- Code duplication
- Missing tests
- Documentation gaps
- Outdated dependencies

**Low (Backlog):**
- Code style improvements
- Refactoring opportunities
- Nice-to-have tooling

**Debt Tracking:**
```javascript
// Add tech debt label to tickets
{
  title: "Refactor task sync logic",
  type: "tech_debt",
  severity: "medium",
  effort: "8 points",
  impact: "Improves maintainability",
  created: "2026-03-15"
}
```

---

## 9.6 Risk Management

### 9.6.1 Technical Risks

**Risk 1: Sync Conflicts**
```
Risk Level: HIGH
Impact: Critical (data loss)
Probability: Medium

Mitigation:
- Implement CRDT (Conflict-free Replicated Data Types)
- Version vectors for conflict detection
- User-friendly conflict resolution UI
- Comprehensive testing
- Rollback capabilities

Contingency:
- Manual conflict resolution
- Data recovery procedures
- User support for conflicts
```

**Risk 2: Mobile App Rejection**
```
Risk Level: MEDIUM
Impact: High (delayed launch)
Probability: Medium

Mitigation:
- Review App Store guidelines thoroughly
- Test on real devices
- Beta testing via TestFlight/Play Console
- Legal review of ToS and Privacy Policy
- Compliance checklist

Contingency:
- Web app priority launch
- Appeal process preparation
- Alternative distribution (TestFlight)
```

**Risk 3: Performance at Scale**
```
Risk Level: MEDIUM
Impact: High (user experience)
Probability: Medium

Mitigation:
- Load testing before launch
- Database indexing strategy
- Caching layer (Redis)
- CDN for static assets
- Auto-scaling infrastructure

Contingency:
- Rate limiting
- Feature flags for degradation
- Horizontal scaling
```

**Risk 4: Third-Party Service Outages**
```
Risk Level: LOW
Impact: Medium
Probability: Low

Mitigation:
- Stripe: Payment retry logic
- Google Calendar: Queue sync jobs
- Email: Multiple providers (SendGrid + AWS SES)
- Monitoring and alerts

Contingency:
- Manual payment processing
- Graceful degradation
- Status page communication
```

### 9.6.2 Business Risks

**Risk 5: Low Conversion Rate**
```
Risk Level: HIGH
Impact: Critical (revenue)
Probability: Medium

Mitigation:
- A/B test pricing
- User research
- Clear value proposition
- Generous free trial
- Usage analytics

Contingency:
- Adjust pricing strategy
- Add more free features
- Introduce bundles earlier
- Extended free trials
```

**Risk 6: High Churn Rate**
```
Risk Level: HIGH
Impact: Critical (growth)
Probability: Medium

Mitigation:
- Onboarding optimization
- Usage monitoring
- Proactive support
- Feature engagement tracking
- Exit surveys

Contingency:
- Win-back campaigns
- Pause subscription option
- Pricing adjustments
- Feature improvements
```

**Risk 7: Competitive Response**
```
Risk Level: MEDIUM
Impact: High
Probability: High

Mitigation:
- Fast execution (time to market)
- Unique positioning (à la carte)
- Strong brand building
- Customer lock-in (data/habits)
- Patent defensive publishing

Contingency:
- Price competition
- Feature differentiation
- Better customer service
- Niche focus
```

### 9.6.3 Team Risks

**Risk 8: Key Person Dependency**
```
Risk Level: MEDIUM
Impact: High
Probability: Low

Mitigation:
- Documentation culture
- Pair programming
- Knowledge sharing sessions
- Cross-training
- Code reviews

Contingency:
- Contractor network
- Recruitment pipeline
- Retention bonuses
```

**Risk 9: Burnout**
```
Risk Level: MEDIUM
Impact: Medium
Probability: Medium

Mitigation:
- Realistic sprint planning
- No weekend work
- PTO encouraged
- Mental health support
- Regular check-ins

Contingency:
- Reduce scope
- Extend timeline
- Hire contractors
```

### 9.6.4 Risk Monitoring

**Weekly Risk Review:**
- Review top 5 risks
- Update probability/impact
- Adjust mitigation strategies
- Escalate as needed

**Risk Dashboard Metrics:**
```
Technical Health:
- Test coverage: >80%
- Build success rate: >95%
- P0 bugs: 0
- P1 bugs: <5

Business Health:
- Conversion rate: >10%
- Churn rate: <5%
- NPS: >40
- Support ticket volume: <100/week

Team Health:
- Sprint velocity: stable
- On-call incidents: <2/week
- Team satisfaction: >7/10
- Turnover: <10%/year
```

```

```

## 10.1 Security Architecture

### 10.1.1 Security Principles

**Security by Design:**
- Defense in depth
- Principle of least privilege
- Zero trust architecture
- Fail securely
- Security awareness

**Security Layers:**
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────┐
│ Application Security                │
│ - Input validation                  │
│ - Output encoding                   │
│ - Authentication/Authorization      │
├─────────────────────────────────────┤
│ API Security                        │
│ - Rate limiting                     │
│ - API key management                │
│ - CORS policies                     │
├─────────────────────────────────────┤
│ Network Security                    │
│ - TLS/SSL encryption                │
│ - VPC isolation                     │
│ - Firewall rules                    │
├─────────────────────────────────────┤
│ Infrastructure Security             │
│ - Container security                │
│ - Secrets management                │
│ - Access controls                   │
├─────────────────────────────────────┤
│ Data Security                       │
│ - Encryption at rest                │
│ - Encryption in transit             │
│ - Backup encryption                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### 10.1.2 Authentication & Authorization

**Authentication Mechanisms:**

**JWT Implementation:**
```typescript
// src/services/auth/jwt.service.ts
import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken';
import { User } from '@/types';

interface TokenPayload {
  userId: string;
  email: string;
  mode: 'individual' | 'enterprise' | 'both';
  enterpriseId?: string;
  roles?: string[];
}

export class JWTService {
  private readonly accessSecret: string;
  private readonly refreshSecret: string;
  
  constructor() {
    this.accessSecret = process.env.JWT_ACCESS_SECRET!;
    this.refreshSecret = process.env.JWT_REFRESH_SECRET!;
  }
  
  generateAccessToken(user: User): string {
    const payload: TokenPayload = {
      userId: user.id,
      email: user.email,
      mode: user.mode,
      enterpriseId: user.enterpriseId,
      roles: user.roles
    };
    
    return jwt.sign(payload, this.accessSecret, {
      expiresIn: '1h',
      issuer: 'prms.io',
      audience: 'prms-api'
    });
  }
  
  generateRefreshToken(userId: string): string {
    return jwt.sign(
      { userId, type: 'refresh' },
      this.refreshSecret,
      { expiresIn: '7d' }
    );
  }
  
  verifyAccessToken(token: string): TokenPayload {
    try {
      return jwt.verify(token, this.accessSecret) as TokenPayload;
    } catch (error) {
      if (error instanceof jwt.TokenExpiredError) {
        throw new AuthError('Token expired');
      }
      throw new AuthError('Invalid token');
    }
  }
  
  verifyRefreshToken(token: string): { userId: string } {
    return jwt.verify(token, this.refreshSecret) as { userId: string };
  }
}
```

**Role-Based Access Control (RBAC):**
```typescript
// src/middleware/authorization.ts
enum Permission {
  // User permissions
  USER_READ = 'user:read',
  USER_WRITE = 'user:write',
  USER_DELETE = 'user:delete',
  
  // Enterprise permissions
  ENTERPRISE_ADMIN = 'enterprise:admin',
  ENTERPRISE_MANAGE_USERS = 'enterprise:manage_users',
  ENTERPRISE_VIEW_ANALYTICS = 'enterprise:view_analytics',
  
  // Project permissions
  PROJECT_CREATE = 'project:create',
  PROJECT_EDIT = 'project:edit',
  PROJECT_DELETE = 'project:delete',
  PROJECT_VIEW = 'project:view'
}

enum Role {
  USER = 'user',
  ENTERPRISE_OWNER = 'enterprise_owner',
  ENTERPRISE_ADMIN = 'enterprise_admin',
  ENTERPRISE_MANAGER = 'enterprise_manager',
  ENTERPRISE_MEMBER = 'enterprise_member'
}

const rolePermissions: Record<Role, Permission[]> = {
  [Role.USER]: [
    Permission.USER_READ,
    Permission.USER_WRITE
  ],
  [Role.ENTERPRISE_OWNER]: [
    Permission.ENTERPRISE_ADMIN,
    Permission.ENTERPRISE_MANAGE_USERS,
    Permission.ENTERPRISE_VIEW_ANALYTICS,
    Permission.PROJECT_CREATE,
    Permission.PROJECT_EDIT,
    Permission.PROJECT_DELETE,
    Permission.PROJECT_VIEW
  ],
  [Role.ENTERPRISE_ADMIN]: [
    Permission.ENTERPRISE_MANAGE_USERS,
    Permission.ENTERPRISE_VIEW_ANALYTICS,
    Permission.PROJECT_CREATE,
    Permission.PROJECT_EDIT,
    Permission.PROJECT_VIEW
  ],
  [Role.ENTERPRISE_MANAGER]: [
    Permission.PROJECT_CREATE,
    Permission.PROJECT_EDIT,
    Permission.PROJECT_VIEW
  ],
  [Role.ENTERPRISE_MEMBER]: [
    Permission.PROJECT_VIEW
  ]
};

export function requirePermission(permission: Permission) {
  return async (req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => {
    const user = req.user; // From auth middleware
    
    if (!user) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
    }
    
    const userPermissions = user.roles.flatMap(
      role => rolePermissions[role] || []
    );
    
    if (!userPermissions.includes(permission)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });
    }
    
    next();
  };
}
```

**Multi-Factor Authentication (2FA):**
```typescript
// src/services/auth/two-factor.service.ts
import speakeasy from 'speakeasy';
import QRCode from 'qrcode';

export class TwoFactorService {
  async generateSecret(email: string): Promise<{
    secret: string;
    qrCode: string;
  }> {
    const secret = speakeasy.generateSecret({
      name: `PrMS (${email})`,
      issuer: 'PrMS'
    });
    
    const qrCode = await QRCode.toDataURL(secret.otpauth_url!);
    
    return {
      secret: secret.base32,
      qrCode
    };
  }
  
  verifyToken(secret: string, token: string): boolean {
    return speakeasy.totp.verify({
      secret,
      encoding: 'base32',
      token,
      window: 2 // Allow 2 time steps tolerance
    });
  }
  
  async enableTwoFactor(
    userId: string,
    secret: string,
    verificationToken: string
  ): Promise<void> {
    if (!this.verifyToken(secret, verificationToken)) {
      throw new Error('Invalid verification token');
    }
    
    await User.updateOne(
      { _id: userId },
      {
        twoFactorEnabled: true,
        twoFactorSecret: secret
      }
    );
  }
}
```

### 10.1.3 API Security

**Rate Limiting:**
```typescript
// src/middleware/rate-limit.ts
import rateLimit from 'express-rate-limit';
import RedisStore from 'rate-limit-redis';
import { redis } from '@/config/redis';

// General API rate limit
export const apiLimiter = rateLimit({
  store: new RedisStore({
    client: redis,
    prefix: 'rl:api:'
  }),
  windowMs: 60 * 1000, // 1 minute
  max: async (req) => {
    const user = req.user;
    
    // Different limits by subscription tier
    if (!user) return 20; // Anonymous
    if (user.tier === 'free') return 100;
    if (user.tier === 'premium') return 500;
    return 2000; // Enterprise
  },
  message: 'Too many requests, please try again later',
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false
});

// Strict limit for authentication endpoints
export const authLimiter = rateLimit({
  store: new RedisStore({
    client: redis,
    prefix: 'rl:auth:'
  }),
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
  max: 5, // 5 attempts
  skipSuccessfulRequests: true,
  message: 'Too many login attempts, please try again later'
});

// Payment endpoints
export const paymentLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 60 * 1000,
  max: 10,
  message: 'Too many payment requests'
});
```

**Input Validation & Sanitization:**
```typescript
// src/middleware/validation.ts
import { body, param, query, validationResult } from 'express-validator';
import DOMPurify from 'isomorphic-dompurify';

export const validateTask = [
  body('title')
    .trim()
    .notEmpty().withMessage('Title is required')
    .isLength({ max: 200 }).withMessage('Title too long')
    .customSanitizer(value => DOMPurify.sanitize(value)),
    
  body('description')
    .optional()
    .trim()
    .isLength({ max: 5000 }).withMessage('Description too long')
    .customSanitizer(value => DOMPurify.sanitize(value)),
    
  body('priority')
    .optional()
    .isIn(['low', 'medium', 'high', 'urgent'])
    .withMessage('Invalid priority'),
    
  body('dueDate')
    .optional()
    .isISO8601().withMessage('Invalid date format')
    .custom((value) => {
      const date = new Date(value);
      if (date < new Date()) {
        throw new Error('Due date must be in the future');
      }
      return true;
    }),
    
  body('tags')
    .optional()
    .isArray().withMessage('Tags must be an array')
    .custom((tags: string[]) => {
      if (tags.length > 10) {
        throw new Error('Maximum 10 tags allowed');
      }
      return tags.every(tag => typeof tag === 'string' && tag.length <= 30);
    })
];

export const handleValidationErrors = (
  req: Request,
  res: Response,
  next: NextFunction
) => {
  const errors = validationResult(req);
  
  if (!errors.isEmpty()) {
    return res.status(422).json({
      success: false,
      error: {
        code: 'VALIDATION_ERROR',
        message: 'Invalid request data',
        details: errors.array()
      }
    });
  }
  
  next();
};
```

**SQL Injection & NoSQL Injection Prevention:**
```typescript
// Using Mongoose with proper sanitization
import mongoSanitize from 'express-mongo-sanitize';

app.use(mongoSanitize({
  replaceWith: '_',
  onSanitize: ({ req, key }) => {
    console.warn(`Sanitized key: ${key}`);
  }
}));

// Safe query construction
async function findTasks(userId: string, filters: any) {
  // BAD - vulnerable to injection
  // const tasks = await Task.find({ userId, ...filters });
  
  // GOOD - sanitized and validated
  const sanitizedFilters = {
    userId: new Types.ObjectId(userId),
    ...(filters.status && { 
      status: { $in: ['not_started', 'in_progress', 'completed'] }
    }),
    ...(filters.priority && {
      priority: { $in: ['low', 'medium', 'high', 'urgent'] }
    })
  };
  
  return Task.find(sanitizedFilters);
}
```

### 10.1.4 Data Encryption

**Encryption at Rest:**
```typescript
// src/services/encryption/encryption.service.ts
import crypto from 'crypto';

export class EncryptionService {
  private readonly algorithm = 'aes-256-gcm';
  private readonly key: Buffer;
  
  constructor() {
    // Key should be stored in secrets manager (AWS Secrets Manager, etc.)
    this.key = Buffer.from(process.env.ENCRYPTION_KEY!, 'hex');
  }
  
  encrypt(data: string): {
    encrypted: string;
    iv: string;
    authTag: string;
  } {
    const iv = crypto.randomBytes(16);
    const cipher = crypto.createCipheriv(this.algorithm, this.key, iv);
    
    let encrypted = cipher.update(data, 'utf8', 'hex');
    encrypted += cipher.final('hex');
    
    const authTag = cipher.getAuthTag();
    
    return {
      encrypted,
      iv: iv.toString('hex'),
      authTag: authTag.toString('hex')
    };
  }
  
  decrypt(encrypted: string, iv: string, authTag: string): string {
    const decipher = crypto.createDecipheriv(
      this.algorithm,
      this.key,
      Buffer.from(iv, 'hex')
    );
    
    decipher.setAuthTag(Buffer.from(authTag, 'hex'));
    
    let decrypted = decipher.update(encrypted, 'hex', 'utf8');
    decrypted += decipher.final('utf8');
    
    return decrypted;
  }
}

// MongoDB field-level encryption
const noteSchema = new Schema({
  userId: { type: ObjectId, required: true },
  title: String,
  content: {
    encrypted: String,
    iv: String,
    authTag: String
  },
  encrypted: { type: Boolean, default: false }
});

noteSchema.pre('save', async function(next) {
  if (this.encrypted && this.isModified('content')) {
    const encryptionService = new EncryptionService();
    const encrypted = encryptionService.encrypt(
      JSON.stringify(this.content)
    );
    this.content = encrypted;
  }
  next();
});
```

**Password Hashing:**
```typescript
// src/services/auth/password.service.ts
import bcrypt from 'bcrypt';

export class PasswordService {
  private readonly saltRounds = 12;
  
  async hash(password: string): Promise<string> {
    return bcrypt.hash(password, this.saltRounds);
  }
  
  async verify(password: string, hash: string): Promise<boolean> {
    return bcrypt.compare(password, hash);
  }
  
  isStrongPassword(password: string): boolean {
    // At least 8 characters
    if (password.length < 8) return false;
    
    // Contains uppercase
    if (!/[A-Z]/.test(password)) return false;
    
    // Contains lowercase
    if (!/[a-z]/.test(password)) return false;
    
    // Contains number
    if (!/[0-9]/.test(password)) return false;
    
    // Contains special character
    if (!/[!@#$%^&*(),.?":{}|<>]/.test(password)) return false;
    
    return true;
  }
}
```

### 10.1.5 Secrets Management

**AWS Secrets Manager Integration:**
```typescript
// src/config/secrets.ts
import {
  SecretsManagerClient,
  GetSecretValueCommand
} from '@aws-sdk/client-secrets-manager';

const client = new SecretsManagerClient({ region: 'us-east-1' });

export async function getSecret(secretName: string): Promise<any> {
  try {
    const response = await client.send(
      new GetSecretValueCommand({ SecretId: secretName })
    );
    
    if (response.SecretString) {
      return JSON.parse(response.SecretString);
    }
    
    throw new Error('Secret not found');
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error retrieving secret:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

// Usage
async function initializeSecrets() {
  const secrets = await getSecret('prms/production/app-secrets');
  
  process.env.JWT_ACCESS_SECRET = secrets.jwtAccessSecret;
  process.env.JWT_REFRESH_SECRET = secrets.jwtRefreshSecret;
  process.env.ENCRYPTION_KEY = secrets.encryptionKey;
  process.env.STRIPE_SECRET_KEY = secrets.stripeSecretKey;
}
```

## 10.2 Data Protection & Privacy

### 10.2.1 Privacy by Design

**Data Minimization:**
- Collect only necessary data
- Clear purpose for each data point
- Regular data retention reviews
- Automatic deletion of old data

**User Control:**
```typescript
// src/services/privacy/data-export.service.ts
export class DataExportService {
  async exportUserData(userId: string): Promise<ExportPackage> {
    const [
      profile,
      tasks,
      events,
      notes,
      transactions,
      habits,
      goals
    ] = await Promise.all([
      User.findById(userId).select('-password -twoFactorSecret'),
      Task.find({ userId }),
      CalendarEvent.find({ userId }),
      Note.find({ userId }),
      Transaction.find({ userId }),
      Habit.find({ userId }),
      Goal.find({ userId })
    ]);
    
    const exportData = {
      exportDate: new Date().toISOString(),
      profile,
      data: {
        tasks,
        events,
        notes,
        transactions,
        habits,
        goals
      },
      metadata: {
        version: '1.0',
        format: 'json'
      }
    };
    
    // Create ZIP file with all data
    const zip = await this.createZipArchive(exportData);
    
    return {
      filename: `prms-data-export-${userId}-${Date.now()}.zip`,
      data: zip
    };
  }
}

// Data deletion service
export class DataDeletionService {
  async deleteUserData(userId: string): Promise<void> {
    // Soft delete - mark as deleted for 30 days grace period
    await User.updateOne(
      { _id: userId },
      {
        status: 'deleted',
        deletedAt: new Date(),
        email: `deleted_${userId}@prms.io`, // Anonymize
        password: null
      }
    );
    
    // Schedule hard deletion after 30 days
    await this.scheduleHardDeletion(userId, 30);
  }
  
  async hardDeleteUserData(userId: string): Promise<void> {
    await Promise.all([
      User.deleteOne({ _id: userId }),
      Task.deleteMany({ userId }),
      CalendarEvent.deleteMany({ userId }),
      Note.deleteMany({ userId }),
      Transaction.deleteMany({ userId }),
      Habit.deleteMany({ userId }),
      Goal.deleteMany({ userId }),
      File.deleteMany({ userId })
    ]);
    
    // Delete from backups
    await this.removeFromBackups(userId);
  }
}
```

### 10.2.2 Data Retention Policy

**Retention Periods:**
```typescript
const retentionPolicies = {
  // Active user data
  activeUserData: 'indefinite', // While account active
  
  // Deleted user data
  softDeletedData: 30, // days
  
  // Activity logs
  activityLogs: 90, // days
  
  // Audit logs
  auditLogs: 365, // days (1 year)
  
  // Backup data
  dailyBackups: 7, // days
  weeklyBackups: 30, // days
  monthlyBackups: 365, // days
  
  // Analytics data
  analyticsRaw: 90, // days
  analyticsAggregated: 730, // days (2 years)
  
  // Payment records
  paymentRecords: 2555, // days (7 years - legal requirement)
};

// Automated cleanup job
async function cleanupExpiredData() {
  const now = new Date();
  
  // Delete soft-deleted users after 30 days
  const deletionThreshold = new Date(now.getTime() - 30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
  const expiredUsers = await User.find({
    status: 'deleted',
    deletedAt: { $lt: deletionThreshold }
  });
  
  for (const user of expiredUsers) {
    await hardDeleteUserData(user._id);
  }
  
  // Clean old activity logs
  const activityThreshold = new Date(now.getTime() - 90 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
  await ActivityLog.deleteMany({ timestamp: { $lt: activityThreshold } });
  
  console.log('Data cleanup completed');
}

// Run daily
cron.schedule('0 2 * * *', cleanupExpiredData);
```

### 10.2.3 Cookie Policy

```typescript
// src/middleware/cookie-consent.ts
import cookieParser from 'cookie-parser';

app.use(cookieParser());

// Cookie categories
enum CookieCategory {
  ESSENTIAL = 'essential',
  FUNCTIONAL = 'functional',
  ANALYTICS = 'analytics',
  MARKETING = 'marketing'
}

const cookieConfig = {
  essential: {
    description: 'Required for basic site functionality',
    cookies: ['session', 'auth_token', 'csrf_token'],
    canDisable: false
  },
  functional: {
    description: 'Remember your preferences',
    cookies: ['theme', 'language', 'timezone'],
    canDisable: true
  },
  analytics: {
    description: 'Help us improve the product',
    cookies: ['_ga', '_gid', 'mixpanel'],
    canDisable: true
  },
  marketing: {
    description: 'Show relevant advertisements',
    cookies: ['fbp', 'ads'],
    canDisable: true
  }
};

// Set cookies based on consent
function setCookie(
  res: Response,
  name: string,
  value: string,
  category: CookieCategory,
  consent: Record<CookieCategory, boolean>
) {
  if (!consent[category] && cookieConfig[category].canDisable) {
    return;
  }
  
  res.cookie(name, value, {
    httpOnly: category === CookieCategory.ESSENTIAL,
    secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production',
    sameSite: 'strict',
    maxAge: category === CookieCategory.ESSENTIAL ? 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000 : 30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000
  });
}
```

## 10.3 Compliance & Regulations

### 10.3.1 GDPR Compliance

**User Rights Implementation:**

**Right to Access:**
```typescript
// GET /api/privacy/data-access
router.get('/privacy/data-access', authenticate, async (req, res) => {
  const userId = req.user.id;
  
  const userData = await DataExportService.exportUserData(userId);
  
  res.json({
    success: true,
    data: {
      personalData: userData.profile,
      dataCategories: Object.keys(userData.data),
      processingPurpose: {
        tasks: 'Task management and productivity tracking',
        events: 'Calendar and scheduling',
        notes: 'Note-taking and knowledge management'
      },
      dataSharing: 'We do not share your data with third parties',
      retentionPeriod: 'Data retained while account is active'
    }
  });
});
```

**Right to Rectification:**
```typescript
// PATCH /api/privacy/update-personal-data
router.patch('/privacy/update-personal-data', authenticate, async (req, res) => {
  const userId = req.user.id;
  const updates = req.body;
  
  // Allow users to update their personal information
  await User.updateOne(
    { _id: userId },
    { $set: updates },
    { runValidators: true }
  );
  
  // Log the rectification
  await AuditLog.create({
    userId,
    action: 'data_rectification',
    details: updates,
    timestamp: new Date()
  });
  
  res.json({ success: true });
});
```

**Right to Erasure (Right to be Forgotten):**
```typescript
// DELETE /api/privacy/delete-account
router.delete('/privacy/delete-account', authenticate, async (req, res) => {
  const userId = req.user.id;
  
  // Soft delete with 30-day grace period
  await DataDeletionService.deleteUserData(userId);
  
  // Send confirmation email
  await sendEmail({
    to: req.user.email,
    subject: 'Account Deletion Scheduled',
    template: 'account-deletion',
    data: {
      gracePeriod: 30,
      recoveryUrl: `${process.env.APP_URL}/recover-account`
    }
  });
  
  res.json({
    success: true,
    message: 'Account will be deleted in 30 days. You can recover it before then.'
  });
});
```

**Right to Data Portability:**
```typescript
// POST /api/privacy/export-data
router.post('/privacy/export-data', authenticate, async (req, res) => {
  const userId = req.user.id;
  const format = req.body.format || 'json'; // json, csv, xml
  
  // Generate export package
  const exportPackage = await DataExportService.exportUserData(userId);
  
  // Convert to requested format
  const data = await convertFormat(exportPackage, format);
  
  // Store in S3 for download
  const downloadUrl = await uploadToS3(data, userId);
  
  // Send download link via email
  await sendEmail({
    to: req.user.email,
    subject: 'Your Data Export is Ready',
    template: 'data-export',
    data: { downloadUrl, expiresIn: '7 days' }
  });
  
  res.json({ success: true, downloadUrl });
});
```

**Right to Object:**
```typescript
// POST /api/privacy/object-processing
router.post('/privacy/object-processing', authenticate, async (req, res) => {
  const userId = req.user.id;
  const { processingType } = req.body; // 'analytics', 'marketing', etc.
  
  await User.updateOne(
    { _id: userId },
    {
      $set: {
        [`consent.${processingType}`]: false
      }
    }
  );
  
  // Stop processing immediately
  await stopProcessing(userId, processingType);
  
  res.json({ success: true });
});
```

### 10.3.3 SOC 2 Compliance Preparation

**Security Controls:**

```typescript
// Audit logging for all sensitive operations
async function auditLog(event: AuditEvent) {
  await AuditLog.create({
    userId: event.userId,
    action: event.action,
    resource: event.resource,
    resourceId: event.resourceId,
    changes: event.changes,
    ipAddress: event.ipAddress,
    userAgent: event.userAgent,
    timestamp: new Date(),
    result: event.result // 'success' | 'failure'
  });
}

// Critical operations that require audit logging
const auditableActions = [
  'user_login',
  'user_logout',
  'password_change',
  'two_factor_enable',
  'two_factor_disable',
  'payment_processed',
  'subscription_created',
  'subscription_cancelled',
  'data_export',
  'data_deletion',
  'admin_action',
  'permission_change'
];

// Middleware to auto-log
export function auditMiddleware(action: string) {
  return async (req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => {
    const originalSend = res.send;
    
    res.send = function(data) {
      auditLog({
        userId: req.user?.id,
        action,
        resource: req.path,
        ipAddress: req.ip,
        userAgent: req.get('user-agent'),
        result: res.statusCode < 400 ? 'success' : 'failure'
      });
      
      return originalSend.call(this, data);
    };
    
    next();
  };
}
```

### 10.4.2 Unit Testing

**Backend Unit Tests:**
```typescript
// src/services/task/task.service.test.ts
import { TaskService } from './task.service';
import { Task } from '@/models/task.model';

describe('TaskService', () => {
  let taskService: TaskService;
  
  beforeEach(() => {
    taskService = new TaskService();
  });
  
  describe('createTask', () => {
    it('should create a task with valid data', async () => {
      const taskData = {
        userId: 'user123',
        title: 'Test Task',
        priority: 'high',
        dueDate: new Date('2026-12-31')
      };
      
      const task = await taskService.createTask(taskData);
      
      expect(task.title).toBe('Test Task');
      expect(task.priority).toBe('high');
      expect(task.status).toBe('not_started');
    });
    
    it('should throw error if title is missing', async () => {
      const taskData = {
        userId: 'user123',
        priority: 'high'
      };
      
      await expect(taskService.createTask(taskData))
        .rejects
        .toThrow('Title is required');
    });
    
    it('should set default priority if not provided', async () => {
      const taskData = {
        userId: 'user123',
        title: 'Test Task'
      };
      
      const task = await taskService.createTask(taskData);
      
      expect(task.priority).toBe('medium');
    });
  });
  
  describe('updateTask', () => {
    it('should update task status', async () => {
      const task = await taskService.createTask({
        userId: 'user123',
        title: 'Test'
      });
      
      const updated = await taskService.updateTask(task.id, {
        status: 'completed'
      });
      
      expect(updated.status).toBe('completed');
      expect(updated.completedAt).toBeDefined();
    });
  });
});
```

**Frontend Unit Tests:**
```typescript
// src/components/TaskList/TaskList.test.tsx
import { render, screen, fireEvent } from '@testing-library/react';
import { TaskList } from './TaskList';

describe('TaskList', () => {
  const mockTasks = [
    { id: '1', title: 'Task 1', status: 'not_started' },
    { id: '2', title: 'Task 2', status: 'completed' }
  ];
  
  it('renders task list correctly', () => {
    render(<TaskList tasks={mockTasks} />);
    
    expect(screen.getByText('Task 1')).toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(screen.getByText('Task 2')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });
  
  it('calls onTaskClick when task is clicked', () => {
    const onTaskClick = jest.fn();
    render(<TaskList tasks={mockTasks} onTaskClick={onTaskClick} />);
    
    fireEvent.click(screen.getByText('Task 1'));
    
    expect(onTaskClick).toHaveBeenCalledWith('1');
  });
  
  it('filters completed tasks', () => {
    render(<TaskList tasks={mockTasks} filter="completed" />);
    
    expect(screen.getByText('Task 2')).toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(screen.queryByText('Task 1')).not.toBeInTheDocument();
  });
});
```

### 10.4.3 Integration Testing

```typescript
// tests/integration/api/tasks.test.ts
import request from 'supertest';
import { app } from '@/app';
import { setupTestDB, cleanupTestDB } from '@/tests/helpers';

describe('Tasks API Integration', () => {
  let authToken: string;
  
  beforeAll(async () => {
    await setupTestDB();
    
    // Create test user and get token
    const response = await request(app)
      .post('/api/auth/register')
      .send({
        email: 'test@example.com',
        password: 'TestPass123!',
        firstName: 'Test',
        lastName: 'User'
      });
    
    authToken = response.body.data.tokens.accessToken;
  });
  
  afterAll(async () => {
    await cleanupTestDB();
  });
  
  describe('POST /api/tasks', () => {
    it('should create a new task', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/tasks')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${authToken}`)
        .send({
          title: 'Integration Test Task',
          priority: 'high',
          dueDate: '2026-12-31T00:00:00Z'
        });
      
      expect(response.status).toBe(201);
      expect(response.body.success).toBe(true);
      expect(response.body.data.title).toBe('Integration Test Task');
    });
    
    it('should return 401 without auth token', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/tasks')
        .send({ title: 'Test' });
      
      expect(response.status).toBe(401);
    });
    
    it('should validate required fields', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/tasks')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${authToken}`)
        .send({ priority: 'high' }); // Missing title
      
      expect(response.status).toBe(422);
      expect(response.body.error.code).toBe('VALIDATION_ERROR');
    });
  });
});
```

test.describe('Complete User Journey', () => {
  test('new user can sign up, create task, and log out', async ({ page }) => {
    // Sign up
    await page.goto('/signup');

    await page.click('[data-testid="new-task-button"]');

    await expect(page).toHaveURL('/login');
  });

    await page.fill('[name="email"]', 'test@example.com');

    // Feature should now be accessible
    await page.goto('/finance');
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="finance-dashboard"]')).toBeVisible();
  });
});

// tests/performance/load-test.ts
import autocannon from 'autocannon';

async function runLoadTest() {
  const result = await autocannon({
    url: 'http://localhost:3000',
    connections: 100,
    duration: 30,
    requests: [
      {
        method: 'GET',
        path: '/api/tasks',
        headers: {
          'Authorization': 'Bearer test-token'
        }
      }
    ]
  });
  
  console.log('Load Test Results:');
  console.log(`Requests/sec: ${result.requests.average}`);
  console.log(`Latency (avg): ${result.latency.mean}ms`);
  console.log(`Latency (p95): ${result.latency.p95}ms`);
  console.log(`Latency (p99): ${result.latency.p99}ms`);
  
  // Assert performance requirements
  if (result.latency.p95 > 200) {
    throw new Error('P95 latency exceeds 200ms requirement');
  }
}

## 10.5 Performance Optimization

### 10.5.1 Database Optimization

**Query Optimization:**
```typescript
// Bad - N+1 query problem
async function getTasksWithProject() {
  const tasks = await Task.find({ userId });
  
  for (const task of tasks) {
    task.project = await Project.findById(task.projectId); // N queries
  }
  
  return tasks;
}

// Good - Use populate
async function getTasksWithProject() {
  return Task.find({ userId })
    .populate('projectId')
    .lean(); // Return plain objects for better performance
}

// Even better - Use aggregation for complex queries
async function getTasksWithStats() {
  return Task.aggregate([
    { $match: { userId: new ObjectId(userId) } },
    {
      $lookup: {
        from: 'projects',
        localField: 'projectId',
        foreignField: '_id',
        as: 'project'
      }
    },
    { $unwind: { path: '$project', preserveNullAndEmptyArrays: true } },
    {
      $group: {
        _id: '$status',
        count: { $sum: 1 },
        tasks: { $push: '$$ROOT' }
      }
    }
  ]);
}
```

**Caching Strategy:**
```typescript
// src/services/cache/cache.service.ts
import Redis from 'ioredis';

export class CacheService {
  private redis: Redis;
  
  constructor() {
    this.redis = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL);
  }
  
  async get<T>(key: string): Promise<T | null> {
    const cached = await this.redis.get(key);
    return cached ? JSON.parse(cached) : null;
  }
  
  async set(key: string, value: any, ttl: number = 3600): Promise<void> {
    await this.redis.setex(key, ttl, JSON.stringify(value));
  }
  
  async del(key: string): Promise<void> {
    await this.redis.del(key);
  }
  
  async invalidatePattern(pattern: string): Promise<void> {
    const keys = await this.redis.keys(pattern);
    if (keys.length > 0) {
      await this.redis.del(...keys);
    }
  }
}

// Usage with decorator
function cached(ttl: number = 3600) {
  return function (
    target: any,
    propertyKey: string,
    descriptor: PropertyDescriptor
  ) {
    const originalMethod = descriptor.value;
    
    descriptor.value = async function (...args: any[]) {
      const cacheKey = `${propertyKey}:${JSON.stringify(args)}`;
      const cache = new CacheService();
      
      const cached = await cache.get(cacheKey);
      if (cached) return cached;
      
      const result = await originalMethod.apply(this, args);
      await cache.set(cacheKey, result, ttl);
      
      return result;
    };
  };
}

// Apply caching
class TaskService {
  @cached(300) // 5 minutes
  async getTasks(userId: string) {
    return Task.find({ userId });
  }
}
```

### 10.5.2 API Optimization

**Response Compression:**
```typescript
import compression from 'compression';

app.use(compression({
  filter: (req, res) => {
    if (req.headers['x-no-compression']) {
      return false;
    }
    return compression.filter(req, res);
  },
  level: 6
}));
```

**Pagination & Cursor-based Loading:**
```typescript
// Cursor-based pagination for better performance on large datasets
router.get('/tasks', async (req, res) => {
  const { cursor, limit = 20 } = req.query;
  
  const query: any = { userId: req.user.id };
  
  if (cursor) {
    query._id = { $gt: new ObjectId(cursor) };
  }
  
  const tasks = await Task.find(query)
    .limit(Number(limit) + 1)
    .sort({ _id: 1 });
  
  const hasMore = tasks.length > Number(limit);
  const results = hasMore ? tasks.slice(0, -1) : tasks;
  const nextCursor = hasMore ? results[results.length - 1]._id : null;
  
  res.json({
    success: true,
    data: results,
    meta: {
      hasMore,
      nextCursor
    }
  });
});
```

### 10.5.3 Frontend Optimization

**Code Splitting:**
```typescript
// src/App.tsx
import { lazy, Suspense } from 'react';

const Dashboard = lazy(() => import('./pages/Dashboard'));
const Tasks = lazy(() => import('./pages/Tasks'));
const Calendar = lazy(() => import('./pages/Calendar'));
const Finance = lazy(() => import('./pages/Finance'));

function App() {
  return (
    <Suspense fallback={<LoadingSpinner />}>
      <Routes>
        <Route path="/dashboard" element={<Dashboard />} />
        <Route path="/tasks" element={<Tasks />} />
        <Route path="/calendar" element={<Calendar />} />
        <Route path="/finance" element={<Finance />} />
      </Routes>
    </Suspense>
  );
}
```

**Virtualization for Large Lists:**
```typescript
// src/components/TaskList/VirtualizedTaskList.tsx
import { FixedSizeList } from 'react-window';

export function VirtualizedTaskList({ tasks }: { tasks: Task[] }) {
  const Row = ({ index, style }: { index: number; style: React.CSSProperties }) => (
    <div style={style}>
      <TaskItem task={tasks[index]} />
    </div>
  );
  
  return (
    <FixedSizeList
      height={600}
      itemCount={tasks.length}
      itemSize={80}
      width="100%"
    >
      {Row}
    </FixedSizeList>
  );
}
```

## 10.6 Monitoring & Logging

### 10.6.1 Application Monitoring

**Health Check Endpoints:**
```typescript
// src/routes/health.ts
router.get('/health', async (req, res) => {
  const checks = await Promise.all([
    checkDatabase(),
    checkRedis(),
    checkS3(),
    checkStripe()
  ]);
  
  const allHealthy = checks.every(check => check.healthy);
  
  res.status(allHealthy ? 200 : 503).json({
    status: allHealthy ? 'healthy' : 'unhealthy',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    checks
  });
});

async function checkDatabase() {
  try {
    await mongoose.connection.db.admin().ping();
    return { service: 'mongodb', healthy: true };
  } catch (error) {
    return { service: 'mongodb', healthy: false, error: error.message };
  }
}
```

**Error Tracking with Sentry:**
```typescript
import * as Sentry from '@sentry/node';

Sentry.init({
  dsn: process.env.SENTRY_DSN,
  environment: process.env.NODE_ENV,
  tracesSampleRate: 0.1,
  beforeSend(event, hint) {
    // Don't send errors for certain paths
    if (event.request?.url?.includes('/health')) {
      return null;
    }
    return event;
  }
});

// Error handling middleware
app.use(Sentry.Handlers.errorHandler());
```

**Metrics with Prometheus:**
```typescript
import promClient from 'prom-client';

const register = new promClient.Registry();

// Default metrics
promClient.collectDefaultMetrics({ register });

// Custom metrics
const httpRequestDuration = new promClient.Histogram({
  name: 'http_request_duration_seconds',
  help: 'Duration of HTTP requests in seconds',
  labelNames: ['method', 'route', 'status_code'],
  buckets: [0.1, 0.5, 1, 2, 5]
});

register.registerMetric(httpRequestDuration);

// Metrics endpoint
app.get('/metrics', async (req, res) => {
  res.set('Content-Type', register.contentType);
  res.end(await register.metrics());
});
```

### 10.6.2 Logging Strategy

**Structured Logging:**
```typescript
import winston from 'winston';

const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp(),
    winston.format.errors({ stack: true }),
    winston.format.json()
  ),
  defaultMeta: {
    service: 'prms-api',
    environment: process.env.NODE_ENV
  },
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.Console({
      format: winston.format.combine(
        winston.format.colorize(),
        winston.format.simple()
      )
    }),
    new winston.transports.File({
      filename: 'logs/error.log',
      level: 'error'
    }),
    new winston.transports.File({
      filename: 'logs/combined.log'
    })
  ]
});

// Usage
logger.info('User logged in', {
  userId: user.id,
  email: user.email,
  ipAddress: req.ip
});

logger.error('Database connection failed', {
  error: error.message,
  stack: error.stack
});
```

## 10.7 Disaster Recovery

### 10.7.1 Backup Strategy

**Automated Backups:**
```typescript
// Daily database backups
import { exec } from 'child_process';
import { S3Client, PutObjectCommand } from '@aws-sdk/client-s3';

async function createDatabaseBackup() {
  const timestamp = new Date().toISOString();
  const backupFile = `backup-${timestamp}.gz`;
  
  // Create MongoDB dump
  await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    exec(
      `mongodump --uri="${process.env.MONGODB_URI}" --archive=${backupFile} --gzip`,
      (error) => {
        if (error) reject(error);
        else resolve(null);
      }
    );
  });
  
  // Upload to S3
  const s3 = new S3Client({ region: 'us-east-1' });
  const fileStream = fs.createReadStream(backupFile);
  
  await s3.send(new PutObjectCommand({
    Bucket: 'prms-backups',
    Key: `daily/${backupFile}`,
    Body: fileStream,
    ServerSideEncryption: 'AES256'
  }));
  
  // Clean up local file
  fs.unlinkSync(backupFile);
  
  logger.info('Database backup completed', { file: backupFile });
}

// Schedule daily at 2 AM
cron.schedule('0 2 * * *', createDatabaseBackup);
```

### 10.7.2 Incident Response

**Incident Response Plan:**

**Severity Levels:**
- **P0 (Critical):** Complete outage, data loss
- **P1 (High):** Major feature broken, security breach
- **P2 (Medium):** Minor feature broken
- **P3 (Low):** Cosmetic issues

**Response Times:**
- P0: Immediate response, 1 hour resolution target
- P1: 15 minute response, 4 hour resolution
- P2: 1 hour response, 24 hour resolution
- P3: Next business day

**Communication Template:**
```typescript
// Incident notification
async function notifyIncident(incident: Incident) {
  const message = `
🚨 INCIDENT ALERT
Severity: ${incident.severity}
Service: ${incident.service}
Description: ${incident.description}
Impact: ${incident.impact}
Status: ${incident.status}
Assigned to: ${incident.assignee}
  `;
  
  // Notify team on Slack
  await slackClient.postMessage('#incidents', message);
  
  // Send PagerDuty alert for P0/P1
  if (incident.severity <= 1) {
    await pagerDuty.trigger({
      incident_key: incident.id,
      description: incident.description
    });
  }
}
```

## Summary

This comprehensive Product Requirements & Analysis document for **PrMS (Productivity Management System)** provides complete specifications across 10 chapters:

1. **Executive Summary** - Vision, personas, value proposition
2. **Individual Features** - 12 features with schemas and pricing
3. **Enterprise Features** - 12 B2B features with workflows
4. **Technical Architecture** - Full system design and tech stack
5. **Database Schemas** - Complete MongoDB schemas with indexes
6. **API Specifications** - RESTful APIs and WebSocket events
7. **UI/UX Design** - Design system, components, user flows
8. **Business Model** - Pricing, revenue projections, competitive analysis
9. **Development Roadmap** - Phases, sprints, milestones
10. **Security & Testing** - Security architecture, compliance, testing strategy

**Total Documentation:** 10 comprehensive chapters ready for implementation.
